id='poem_sentence_299_1364236_comment'></div>山栖乌鸟。水宿鸳鸯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1364236_comment'></div>蜀门荷戟。江津滥觞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1364236_comment'></div>落星高堰。明月回塘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1364236_comment'></div>丹碑不朽。清庙无疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1364236_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_304_1364236_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=675&endYear=675')">675年</a>　冬,应制举及第,补官校书郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=676&endYear=676')">676年</a>　为弘文馆校书郎.作《唐上骑都尉高君神道碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷8第127页。）</span><div id='poem_1364244' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364244' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364244?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐上骑都尉高君神道碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（676年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364244")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364244_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364244'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364244'>南方火德。阳精赫雷电之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364244_comment'></div>西陆金行。秋令毒风霜之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364244_comment'></div>达其变。圣人所以定天下之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364244_comment'></div>象其宜。圣人所以观天下之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364244_comment'></div>或衣裳六合。舞干戚而扫虔刘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364244_comment'></div>或钟鼓八纮。用甲兵而诛暴乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364244_comment'></div>若夫皇天失纪。彗孛飞流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364244_comment'></div>后土不纲。山河崩竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364244_comment'></div>蚩尤食石。灾害于生人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364244_comment'></div>项羽拔山。凭陵于上国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364244_comment'></div>天子闻鼓鼙之响。思将帅以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1364244", 1364244, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>龚行</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364244_comment'></div>将军属甲冑之容。揽英雄而决胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364244_comment'></div>则风云潜感。豪杰挺生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364244_comment'></div>得七星之武曲破军。受五运之金多木少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364244_comment'></div>四时繁弱。射连尹于嶅山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364244_comment'></div>万辟太阿。杀颜良于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1364244", 1364244, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>官渡</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364244_comment'></div>然后达人知足。徒兴白发之歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364244_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364244", 1364244, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>烈士</span>徇名。不受黄金之赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364244_comment'></div>与夫弃其笔墨。汉家封万里之侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364244_comment'></div>称尔戈矛。周王命百夫之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364244_comment'></div>岂可同年而语哉。君讳则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364244_comment'></div>字宏规。其先渤海人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364244_comment'></div>后代因官。遂家于泾州之安定县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364244_comment'></div>神房阿阁。泰山横日观之峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364244_comment'></div>金阙银台。沧海蔽天虚之岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364244_comment'></div>风土形胜。关河表里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364244_comment'></div>三分六州之大业。师尚父赞其经纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364244_comment'></div>一匡九合之元勋。齐桓公拓其疆场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364244_comment'></div>高柴至德。藉东鲁之声名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364244_comment'></div>高凤沈研。盛西京之学校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364244_comment'></div>英才磊落而秀发。人物蝉联而间起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364244_comment'></div>三光不坠。察高星于太紫之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364244_comment'></div>八柱无疆。奠高岳于中黄之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364244_comment'></div>曾祖冲。北齐鹰扬郎将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364244_comment'></div>周左屯卫清宫府别将。成军夜火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364244_comment'></div>教战秋风。九天扬后一之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364244_comment'></div>六合拥前三之阵。张良入汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364244_comment'></div>行观灭楚之徵。微子奔周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364244_comment'></div>坐见亡殷之兆。祖赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364244_comment'></div>周褒郡南和县长。陶元亮摄官于彭泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364244_comment'></div>道契羲皇。陈仲弓历职于太邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364244_comment'></div>德符星纬。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1364244", 1364244, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>飘风骤雨</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364244_comment'></div>不入灌坛之乡。暴虎苍鹰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364244_comment'></div>潜出瑕邱之境。考才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364244_comment'></div>朝议郎上开府。孙子荆之天骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364244_comment'></div>亮拔不群。王夷甫之道心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364244_comment'></div>神锋太峻。议郎清秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364244_comment'></div>悬符处士之星。开府崇班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364244_comment'></div>上接台阶之位。君雄心独断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364244_comment'></div>猛气无前。用兵书六甲于自然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364244_comment'></div>知射法三篇于性道。早图星象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364244_comment'></div>管公明怀察变之心。幼识旌旗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364244_comment'></div>陶恭祖有行师之略。属隋人板荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364244_comment'></div>天下崩离。朱阳夹飞鸟之云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364244_comment'></div>紫极现雄鸡之象。陈兵争战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364244_comment'></div>窥玉策于中州。姚石坛场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364244_comment'></div>窃金符于宇县。我高祖黄云大帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364244_comment'></div>白水真人。风雷海岳之纯精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364244_comment'></div>天地阴阳之正气。娲皇受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364244_comment'></div>杀<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_59_1364244", 1364244, "Clauses/118/Comments/0")'>黑龙</span>而定水灾。汉祖乘机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364244_comment'></div>斩白蛇而开火运。君夜观乾象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364244_comment'></div>昼察人情。审荧惑之歌谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364244_comment'></div>验嵩山之谶记。关中王气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364244_comment'></div>不劳甘德之言。沛国真星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364244_comment'></div>无待殷馗之说。贼薛举豺狼枭獍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364244_comment'></div>梼杌穷奇。守幽陇以行灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364244_comment'></div>负关河而作孽。天王按剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364244_comment'></div>出军于玉帐之前。猛将分麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364244_comment'></div>受律于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_68_1364244", 1364244, "Clauses/136/Comments/0")'>金坛</span>之下。以义宁二年王师薄伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364244_comment'></div>赵国公长孙无忌精兵若兽。利器如霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364244_comment'></div>问君以帷幄之谋。待君以心腹之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364244_comment'></div>营当月晕。因八门之死生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364244_comment'></div>阵法天星。乘五将之关格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364244_comment'></div>荫华盖。历明堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364244_comment'></div>以我和而制其离。以我直而摧其曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364244_comment'></div>败楚师于柏举。未足权衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364244_comment'></div>执秦俘于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_76_1364244", 1364244, "Clauses/152/Comments/0")'>崤陵</span>。无阶等级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364244_comment'></div>此实君之功也。其年诏授朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364244_comment'></div>赐物三百段。排患而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_78_1364244", 1364244, "Clauses/157/Comments/0")'>释滞</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364244_comment'></div>功成而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_79_1364244", 1364244, "Clauses/158/Comments/0")'>不居</span>。比疏傅而辞荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364244_comment'></div>追留侯以高蹈。三灵革故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364244_comment'></div>君子于焉待时。四海清平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364244_comment'></div>谋臣以之归第。自太王基命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364244_comment'></div>成康隆玉版之图。高帝受终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364244_comment'></div>文武盛金刀之业。家给人足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364244_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_85_1364244", 1364244, "Clauses/170/Comments/0")'>天成地平</span>。犹劳水旱之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364244_comment'></div>尚想京坻之积。咸亨三年春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364244_comment'></div>奉敕于河阳检校水运使。搜粟都尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364244_comment'></div>河堤使者。铜桡铁舳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364244_comment'></div>苍鹰白鹤之船。竹箭桃花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364244_comment'></div>贝阙龙堂之水。引红粟于淮海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364244_comment'></div>汎归舟于秦晋。遂使齐臣献纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364244_comment'></div>先陈不涸之名。汉后丝纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364244_comment'></div>即有常平之号。望千石之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364244_comment'></div>可以疗饥。开万箱之储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364244_comment'></div>自然知礼。此又君之功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364244_comment'></div>其年诏赐上骑都尉。嗟夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364244_comment'></div>河流曲直。天道盈虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364244_comment'></div>鬼神莫之要。圣贤莫能预。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364244_comment'></div>高台下泣。孟尝君之恻怆可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364244_comment'></div>梁木兴歌。孔宣父之平生巳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364244_comment'></div>上元三年春三月日。终于乐邑里之私第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364244_comment'></div>享年七十六。惟君魁梧动俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364244_comment'></div>符彩惊人。忠孝天资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364244_comment'></div>温良日用。一门兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364244_comment'></div>尽同钟毓之车。千里宾朋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364244_comment'></div>时命嵇康之驾。每至白云生海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364244_comment'></div>素月流天。未尝不顾盼山河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364244_comment'></div>抑扬琴酒。冯异之大树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364244_comment'></div>对诸将而无言。子夏之名山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364244_comment'></div>谢时人以长往。四林<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_110_1364244", 1364244, "Clauses/221/Comments/0")'>游刃</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364244_comment'></div>八水忘筌。能袪有漏之因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364244_comment'></div>早得无生之法。虽十年俱尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364244_comment'></div>陆士衡之长叹有徵。而千戴犹生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364244_comment'></div>蔺相如之壮心恒在。即以冬十月丁酉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364244_comment'></div>葬于安定东南二十里之平原。礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364244_comment'></div>陶公相宅。郭璞占坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364244_comment'></div>面丹凤而背元龟。兆青乌而徵白马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364244_comment'></div>三百篇之后。卜筮何从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364244_comment'></div>二千石之荣。子孙无替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364244_comment'></div>长男仁睿中男仁楷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_120_1364244", 1364244, "Clauses/240/Comments/0")'>少男</span>仁护仁昉等。或体穷三变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364244_comment'></div>潘陆不足以升堂。或力敌万夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364244_comment'></div>关张不足以扶毂。有元方季方之长幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364244_comment'></div>传学诗学礼之门风。金友玉昆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364244_comment'></div>忠臣孝子。穷号积于心髓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364244_comment'></div>创钜缠于肌骨。星辰巳变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364244_comment'></div>昊天无报德之期。霜露潜移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364244_comment'></div>君子有终身之感。葬之以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364244_comment'></div>垂制度于三王。思之以时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364244_comment'></div>别蒸尝于四季。然后按韦贤之旧德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364244_comment'></div>叙潘岳之家风。戴逵铭北海之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364244_comment'></div>张昶刻西山之石。若使邓将军之一见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364244_comment'></div>自得嘉名。魏太祖之来观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364244_comment'></div>悬知绝唱。其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364244_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_134_1364244'>金阙千仞。银宫百常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364244_comment'></div>发挥雷雨。震动阴阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364244_comment'></div>山水形胜。人神会昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364244_comment'></div>九州霸业。赐履勤王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364244_comment'></div>乐只君子。邦家之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364244_comment'></div>惊雷气候。大昴徵祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364244_comment'></div>运属飞海。时逢吸霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364244_comment'></div>中原逐鹿。西岳亡羊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364244_comment'></div>汉起高帝。周兴太王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364244_comment'></div>乃披荆棘。即奉坛场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364244_comment'></div>国步犹阻。黎元未康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364244_comment'></div>将军不拜。使者相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364244_comment'></div>阵合星斗。兵符玉璜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364244_comment'></div>歼夷叛逆。刷涤边荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364244_comment'></div>化穆三代。时清九皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364244_comment'></div>犹思礼节。尚试尧汤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364244_comment'></div>漕通淮海。水泛舟航。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364244_comment'></div>苍鹰鹢轴。紫贝龙堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364244_comment'></div>功立身退。悬车杖乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364244_comment'></div>百年俄顷。万绪悲凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364244_comment'></div>昔时华屋。今日元房。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364244_comment'></div>平天惨惨。半月苍苍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364244_comment'></div>地谓西郭。山言北邙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364244_comment'></div>曲池无处。松槚成行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364244_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_158_1364244_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=676&endYear=676')">676年</a>　为弘文馆校书郎.作《彭城公夫人尔朱氏墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷10第183页。）</span><div id='poem_1364258' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364258' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364258?labeling=true' target='_blank'>彭城公夫人尔朱氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（676年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364258")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364258_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364258'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364258'>夫人尔朱氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364258_comment'></div>河南洛阳人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364258_comment'></div>若夫阴山表里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364258_comment'></div>冲北斗之玑衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364258_comment'></div>瀚海弥纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364258_comment'></div>直西街之毕昴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364258_comment'></div>四时衔火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364258_comment'></div>烛龙开照地之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364258_comment'></div>六月抟风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364258_comment'></div>大鹏运垂天之翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364258_comment'></div>由是奄有京县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364258_comment'></div>遂荒中土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364258_comment'></div>车书礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364258_comment'></div>三王之损益可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364258_comment'></div>将相公侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364258_comment'></div>百代之山河不殒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364258_comment'></div>祖敞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364258_comment'></div>隋仪同三司金紫光禄大夫岐同金申信临徐七州总管兵部尚书金城郡开国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364258_comment'></div>天列尚书之星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364258_comment'></div>地标光禄之塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364258_comment'></div>出身万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364258_comment'></div>知吕岱之元勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364258_comment'></div>专命一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364258_comment'></div>识刘宏之重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364258_comment'></div>父休最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364258_comment'></div>隋左千牛备身朝散大夫齐王府司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364258_comment'></div>袭封爵金城公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364258_comment'></div>大夫称伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364258_comment'></div>诸侯胙土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364258_comment'></div>淮仙致雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364258_comment'></div>仍攀桂树之山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364258_comment'></div>楚客临风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364258_comment'></div>更入芙蓉之水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364258_comment'></div>夫人玉台贞气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364258_comment'></div>金河仙液。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364258_comment'></div>蔡中郎之女子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364258_comment'></div>早听色丝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364258_comment'></div>谢太傅之闺门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364258_comment'></div>先扬丽则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364258_comment'></div>彭城公发源殷伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364258_comment'></div>承家汉相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364258_comment'></div>山川气候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364258_comment'></div>彰白虎于皋陶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364258_comment'></div>象纬休徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364258_comment'></div>下苍龙于曼倩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364258_comment'></div>三星照夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364258_comment'></div>伫稽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1364258", 1364258, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>鸣雁</span>之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364258_comment'></div>七日秉秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364258_comment'></div>坐荐飞皇之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364258_comment'></div>夫人年甫十八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364258_comment'></div>遂归于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364258_comment'></div>巫山南眺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364258_comment'></div>逢暮雨于瑶姬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364258_comment'></div>华岳西临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364258_comment'></div>降明星于玉女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364258_comment'></div>动合诗礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364258_comment'></div>言成轨则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364258_comment'></div>晨昏展敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364258_comment'></div>事极于移天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364258_comment'></div>蘋藻挈诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364258_comment'></div>义申于中馈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364258_comment'></div>女郎砧石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364258_comment'></div>响明月而思秋风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364258_comment'></div>织妇机床。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364258_comment'></div>听寒蛩而催络纬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364258_comment'></div>用曹大家之明训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364258_comment'></div>执宋伯姬之贞节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364258_comment'></div>加以心依八觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364258_comment'></div>理会三空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364258_comment'></div>游智刃于檀林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364258_comment'></div>泛仙舟于法海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364258_comment'></div>几神独照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364258_comment'></div>默言象而无施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364258_comment'></div>空有兼忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364258_comment'></div>束筌蹄而不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364258_comment'></div>人生天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364258_comment'></div>寿非金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364258_comment'></div>银台窃药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364258_comment'></div>想奔月而何年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364258_comment'></div>金殿煎香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364258_comment'></div>思反魂而无日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364258_comment'></div>以某年月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364258_comment'></div>终于平原里之私第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364258_comment'></div>越上元三年十月二十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364258_comment'></div>合葬于城南之毕原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364258_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364258_comment'></div>齐侯寝侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364258_comment'></div>杜氏阶前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364258_comment'></div>对文王之毕原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364258_comment'></div>用周公之合葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364258_comment'></div>偃松千古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364258_comment'></div>长无寡鹤之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364258_comment'></div>文梓百寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364258_comment'></div>还见<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_93_1364258", 1364258, "Clauses/93/Comments/0")'>双鸳</span>之集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364258_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364258_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_95_1364258'>合葬非古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364258_comment'></div>周公所存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364258_comment'></div>死生千载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364258_comment'></div>棺椁双魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364258_comment'></div>野旷风急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364258_comment'></div>天寒日昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364258_comment'></div>烟霾杳嶂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364258_comment'></div>雾失遥村。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364258_comment'></div>纪黄绢之碑表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364258_comment'></div>对青松之墓门。</div><div id='poem_sentence_104_1364258_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=677&endYear=677')">677年1月30日</a>　为弘文馆校书郎.春正月晦日,与友人郊游,作《晦日药园诗序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷3第45页。）</span><div id='poem_1364199' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364199' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364199?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晦日药园诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（677年1月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364199")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364199_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364199'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364199'>天下皆知礼之为贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364199_comment'></div>用周旋揖让之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364199_comment'></div>天下皆知乐之为盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364199_comment'></div>节金石丝簧之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364199_comment'></div>是则忠信之薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364199_comment'></div>饰容貌于矜庄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364199_comment'></div>风俗之微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364199_comment'></div>陶性灵于歌舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364199_comment'></div>殊不知达人君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364199_comment'></div>遗形骸于得丧之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364199_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1364199", 1364199, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>心照神交</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364199_comment'></div>混荣辱于是非之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364199_comment'></div>非若诸公者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364199_comment'></div>大夫之相知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364199_comment'></div>以为烟霞可赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364199_comment'></div>岁月难留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364199_comment'></div>遂欲极千载之交欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364199_comment'></div>穷百年之乐事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364199_comment'></div>莫不如圭如璋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364199_comment'></div>令闻令望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364199_comment'></div>济济锵锵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364199_comment'></div>同会于文场者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364199_comment'></div>于时丁丑之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364199_comment'></div>孟春之晦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364199_comment'></div>岁阴入于星纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364199_comment'></div>斗柄临于析木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364199_comment'></div>衣冠杂沓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364199_comment'></div>出城阙而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1364199", 1364199, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>盘游</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364199_comment'></div>车马骈阗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364199_comment'></div>俯河演而帐饮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364199_comment'></div>乃有神州<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1364199", 1364199, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>福地</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364199_comment'></div>上药中园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364199_comment'></div>左太冲所云当衢向术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364199_comment'></div>潘安仁以为面郊后韨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364199_comment'></div>九茎仙草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364199_comment'></div>摇八卦之祥风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364199_comment'></div>四照<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1364199", 1364199, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>灵葩</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364199_comment'></div>泫三危之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1364199", 1364199, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>宝露</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364199_comment'></div>岂直帝神农旋赤鞭而驱毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364199_comment'></div>崔文子拥朱幡以救人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364199_comment'></div>山图采之而得道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364199_comment'></div>姮娥窃之而奔月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364199_comment'></div>若斯而已哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364199_comment'></div>加以回溪漱石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364199_comment'></div>茂林脩竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364199_comment'></div>澹风日之逶迤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364199_comment'></div>妙山泉之体势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364199_comment'></div>然后搴杜若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364199_comment'></div>藉芝兰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364199_comment'></div>高论参元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364199_comment'></div>飞触举白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364199_comment'></div>凡我良友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364199_comment'></div>同声相应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364199_comment'></div>心冥宠辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364199_comment'></div>推富贵于皇天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364199_comment'></div>事一穷通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364199_comment'></div>任运随于大命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364199_comment'></div>若使适情知足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364199_comment'></div>则玉帛子女为伐性之源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364199_comment'></div>达变通机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364199_comment'></div>则尊官厚禄非保全之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364199_comment'></div>所以列坐羲皇之代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364199_comment'></div>安歌帝尧之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364199_comment'></div>阳光稍晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364199_comment'></div>高兴未阑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364199_comment'></div>请诸<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1364199", 1364199, "Clauses/65/Comments/0")'>文会</span>之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364199_comment'></div>共纪当年之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364199_comment'></div>凡厥众作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364199_comment'></div>列之于后。</div><div id='poem_sentence_68_1364199_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=677&endYear=677')">677年</a>　为弘文馆校书郎.上《公卿以下冕服议》,驳斥太常博士苏知几等人请改冕服图案的建议,朝廷予以采纳。<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷5第75页。）</span><div id='poem_1364193' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364193' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364193?labeling=true' target='_blank'>公卿以下冕服议</a><span class='authorDate'>（677年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364193")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364193_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364193'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364193'>古者太昊庖牺氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364193_comment'></div>仰以观象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364193_comment'></div>俯以察法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364193_comment'></div>造书契而文籍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364193_comment'></div>次有黄帝轩辕氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364193_comment'></div>长而敦敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364193_comment'></div>成而聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364193_comment'></div>垂衣裳而天下理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364193_comment'></div>其后数迁五德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364193_comment'></div>君非一姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364193_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1364193", 1364193, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>体国经野</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364193_comment'></div>建邦设都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364193_comment'></div>文质所以再而复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364193_comment'></div>正朔所以三而改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364193_comment'></div>夫改正朔者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364193_comment'></div>谓夏后氏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1364193", 1364193, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>建寅</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364193_comment'></div>殷人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364193", 1364193, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>建丑</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364193_comment'></div>周人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364193", 1364193, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>建子</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364193_comment'></div>至于以日系月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364193_comment'></div>以月系时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364193_comment'></div>以时系年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364193_comment'></div>此则三王相袭之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364193_comment'></div>夫易服色者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364193_comment'></div>谓夏后氏尚黑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364193_comment'></div>殷人尚白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364193_comment'></div>周人尚赤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364193_comment'></div>至于山龙<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1364193", 1364193, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>华虫</span>宗彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364193_comment'></div>藻火粉米黼黻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364193_comment'></div>此又百代可知之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364193_comment'></div>今苏知机表奏请立节文改章服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364193_comment'></div>奉付礼官学士详定是非者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364193_comment'></div>谨按虞书曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364193_comment'></div>予欲观<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1364193", 1364193, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>古人</span>之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364193_comment'></div>日月星辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364193_comment'></div>山龙<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1364193", 1364193, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>华虫</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364193_comment'></div>作会宗彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364193_comment'></div>藻火粉米。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364193_comment'></div>黼黻絺绣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364193_comment'></div>由此言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364193_comment'></div>则其所从来者尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364193_comment'></div>夫日月星辰者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364193_comment'></div>象圣王光照下土也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364193_comment'></div>山者布散云雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364193_comment'></div>象圣王泽沾下人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364193_comment'></div>龙者变化无方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364193_comment'></div>象圣王应时布教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364193_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1364193", 1364193, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>华虫</span>者雉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364193_comment'></div>身被五彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364193_comment'></div>象圣王体兼文明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364193_comment'></div>宗彝者虎蜼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364193_comment'></div>以刚猛制物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364193_comment'></div>象圣王神武定乱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364193_comment'></div>藻者逐水上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364193_comment'></div>象圣王随代而应也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364193_comment'></div>火者陶冶烹饪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364193_comment'></div>象圣王至德日新也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364193_comment'></div>粉米者人恃以生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364193_comment'></div>象圣王为物之所赖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364193_comment'></div>黼者能断割。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364193_comment'></div>象圣王临事能决也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364193_comment'></div>黻者两已相背。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364193_comment'></div>象君臣可否相济也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364193_comment'></div>逮有周氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364193_comment'></div>乃以日月星辰为旌旗之饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364193_comment'></div>又登龙于山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364193_comment'></div>登火于宗彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364193_comment'></div>尊神明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364193_comment'></div>于是乎制衮冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364193_comment'></div>以祀先王也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364193_comment'></div>九章者法阳数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364193_comment'></div>以龙为首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364193_comment'></div>章衮者卷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364193_comment'></div>龙德神异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364193_comment'></div>应变潜见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364193_comment'></div>表圣王深识远知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364193_comment'></div>卷舒神化也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364193_comment'></div>又制鷩冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364193_comment'></div>以祭先公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364193_comment'></div>鷩者雉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364193_comment'></div>有耿介之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364193_comment'></div>表公有贤才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364193_comment'></div>能守耿介之节也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364193_comment'></div>又制毳冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364193_comment'></div>以祭四望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364193_comment'></div>四望者岳渎之神也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364193_comment'></div>虎蜼者山林所生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364193_comment'></div>明其象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364193_comment'></div>又制絺冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364193_comment'></div>以祭社稷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364193_comment'></div>社稷者土谷之神也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364193_comment'></div>粉米由之而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364193_comment'></div>象其功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364193_comment'></div>又制元冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364193_comment'></div>以祭群小祀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364193_comment'></div>百神异形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364193_comment'></div>难可遍拟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364193_comment'></div>但取黻之相背。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364193_comment'></div>昭异名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364193_comment'></div>夫以周公之多才也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364193_comment'></div>故治定制礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364193_comment'></div>功成作乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364193_comment'></div>夫以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_101_1364193", 1364193, "Clauses/101/Comments/0")'>孔宣</span>之将圣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364193_comment'></div>故行夏之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364193_comment'></div>服周之冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364193_comment'></div>先王之法服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364193_comment'></div>乃此之自出矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364193_comment'></div>天下之服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364193_comment'></div>能事又于是乎毕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364193_comment'></div>今知机表状请制大明冕十二章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364193_comment'></div>乘舆服之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364193_comment'></div>谨按日月星辰者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364193_comment'></div>已施于旌旗矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364193_comment'></div>龙山火米者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364193_comment'></div>又不踰于古矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364193_comment'></div>而云麟凤有四灵之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364193_comment'></div>元龟有负图之应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364193_comment'></div>云有纪官之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364193_comment'></div>水有盛德之祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364193_comment'></div>此盖别表休徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364193_comment'></div>终是无所比象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364193_comment'></div>然则皇王受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364193_comment'></div>天地兴符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364193_comment'></div>仰观则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_122_1364193", 1364193, "Clauses/122/Comments/0")'>璧合珠连</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364193_comment'></div>俯察则银黄<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_123_1364193", 1364193, "Clauses/123/Comments/0")'>玉紫</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364193_comment'></div>尽南宫之粉墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364193_comment'></div>不足写其行状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364193_comment'></div>罄东观之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_126_1364193", 1364193, "Clauses/126/Comments/0")'>铅黄</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364193_comment'></div>无以纪其名实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364193_comment'></div>固不可毕施于法服也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364193_comment'></div>云也者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364193_comment'></div>从龙之气也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364193_comment'></div>水也者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364193_comment'></div>藻之自生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364193_comment'></div>又不假别为章目也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364193_comment'></div>此盖不经之甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364193_comment'></div>又<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_135_1364193", 1364193, "Clauses/135/Comments/0")'>鸾冕</span>八章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364193_comment'></div>三公服之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364193_comment'></div>鸾者太平之瑞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364193_comment'></div>非三公之德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364193_comment'></div>鹰鹯者鸷鸟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364193_comment'></div>适可以辨刑曹之职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364193_comment'></div>熊罴者猛兽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364193_comment'></div>适可以旌武臣之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364193_comment'></div>又称藻为水草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364193_comment'></div>而无法象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364193_comment'></div>引张衡赋云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364193_comment'></div>蒂倒茄于藻井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364193_comment'></div>被红葩之狎猎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364193_comment'></div>谓为莲华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364193_comment'></div>取其文彩者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364193_comment'></div>夫茄者莲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364193_comment'></div>藻者饰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364193_comment'></div>盖以莲饰井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364193_comment'></div>非谓藻为莲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364193_comment'></div>若以莲代藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364193_comment'></div>变古从今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364193_comment'></div>既不知草木之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364193_comment'></div>亦未达文章之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364193_comment'></div>此又不经之甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364193_comment'></div>又毳冕六章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364193_comment'></div>三品服之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364193_comment'></div>按此王者祀四望服之名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364193_comment'></div>今三品乃得同王之毳冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364193_comment'></div>而三公不得同王之衮名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364193_comment'></div>岂惟颠倒衣裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364193_comment'></div>抑亦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_165_1364193", 1364193, "Clauses/165/Comments/0")'>自相矛盾</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364193_comment'></div>此又不经之甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364193_comment'></div>又黼冕四章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364193_comment'></div>五品服之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364193_comment'></div>考之于古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364193_comment'></div>则无其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364193_comment'></div>验之于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364193_comment'></div>则非章首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364193_comment'></div>此又不经之甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364193_comment'></div>国家以断鳌鍊石之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364193_comment'></div>今上以纬地经天之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364193_comment'></div>汉称文景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364193_comment'></div>周曰成康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364193_comment'></div>讲八代之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364193_comment'></div>蒐三王之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364193_comment'></div>文物既行矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364193_comment'></div>尊卑又明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364193_comment'></div>天下已和平矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364193_comment'></div>万国巳咸宁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364193_comment'></div>诚请顺考古道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364193_comment'></div>率由旧章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364193_comment'></div>弗询之谋勿庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364193_comment'></div>无稽之言勿听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364193_comment'></div>若夫礼惟从俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364193_comment'></div>则命为制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364193_comment'></div>令为诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364193_comment'></div>乃秦皇之故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364193_comment'></div>犹可以适于今矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364193_comment'></div>若夫义取随时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364193_comment'></div>则出称警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364193_comment'></div>入称跸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364193_comment'></div>乃汉国之旧仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364193_comment'></div>犹可以行于代矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364193_comment'></div>亦何取于变周公之轨物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364193_comment'></div>改宣尼之法度者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364193_comment'></div>谨议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_200_1364193_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=678&endYear=678')">678年</a>　为弘文馆校书郎.作《从甥梁锜墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷9第155页。）</span><div id='poem_1364252' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364252' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364252?labeling=true' target='_blank'>从甥梁锜墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（678年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364252")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364252_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364252'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364252'>故右卫率府翊卫安定梁锜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364252_comment'></div>年二十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364252_comment'></div>以上元三年秋八月某日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364252_comment'></div>终于某所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364252_comment'></div>图其景宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364252_comment'></div>天有大梁之星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364252_comment'></div>辨其物土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364252_comment'></div>地有大梁之物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364252_comment'></div>考其衣冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364252_comment'></div>人有大梁之姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364252_comment'></div>综乾坤而列位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364252_comment'></div>兼水木而成文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364252_comment'></div>业耕织而乐琴书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364252_comment'></div>有梁鸿之雅尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364252_comment'></div>生封侯而死庙食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364252_comment'></div>有梁竦之雄图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364252_comment'></div>西山求白鹿之仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364252_comment'></div>东海受黄蛇之宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364252_comment'></div>曾祖某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364252_comment'></div>光禄大夫开府仪同三司骠骑将军清河太守右卫大将军同州刺史上柱国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364252_comment'></div>郡守旁通于月建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364252_comment'></div>仪同上法于太阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364252_comment'></div>光禄大夫下大夫之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364252_comment'></div>骠骑将军大将军之比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364252_comment'></div>祖其。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364252_comment'></div>河南渑池令郑州司功参军事冀州蒲州二府司马朝散大夫纪王府司马襄州同州二长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364252_comment'></div>仲由宰邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364252_comment'></div>萧何主吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364252_comment'></div>桓温之徵谢奕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364252_comment'></div>暂为司马之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364252_comment'></div>周景之礼陈蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364252_comment'></div>仍降<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1364252", 1364252, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>题舆</span>之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364252_comment'></div>考某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364252_comment'></div>国子学生霍王府参军并州大都督府兵曹扬州大都督府录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364252_comment'></div>仲尼闲居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364252_comment'></div>曰参不敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364252_comment'></div>天子命我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364252_comment'></div>参卿军事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364252_comment'></div>张常山之福应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364252_comment'></div>直保金钩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364252_comment'></div>谢太傅之闺门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364252_comment'></div>唯生玉树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364252_comment'></div>所以圆光折水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364252_comment'></div>真气冲天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364252_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1364252", 1364252, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>孩笑</span>之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364252_comment'></div>见之者知其孝友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364252_comment'></div>能言之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364252_comment'></div>听之者许其聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364252_comment'></div>审清河<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1364252", 1364252, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>管辂</span>之天文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364252_comment'></div>对江夏黄童之日蚀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364252_comment'></div>挥其劲翮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364252_comment'></div>则凤凰飞鸣于赤山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364252_comment'></div>整其兰䈥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364252_comment'></div>则骏马腾骧于绿地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364252_comment'></div>若夫龙神负卦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364252_comment'></div>瑞雀衔书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364252_comment'></div>安釐王汲冢之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364252_comment'></div>穆天子羽陵之籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364252_comment'></div>莫不因条报叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364252_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_59_1364252", 1364252, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>望表知里</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364252_comment'></div>郑元殚见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364252_comment'></div>览万卷之八千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364252_comment'></div>班固<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_1364252", 1364252, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>洽闻</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364252_comment'></div>涉五经之四部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364252_comment'></div>至如雕弧夜月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364252_comment'></div>䈥角三材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364252_comment'></div>铁剑秋霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364252_comment'></div>烟云五色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364252_comment'></div>莫不推之以智勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364252_comment'></div>成之以揖让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364252_comment'></div>历诸侯而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1364252", 1364252, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>说剑</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364252_comment'></div>直之无前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364252_comment'></div>引司马而操弓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364252_comment'></div>观者如堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364252_comment'></div>可谓多才天纵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364252_comment'></div>盛德日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364252_comment'></div>曼倩不让于诗书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364252_comment'></div>翁归兼强于文武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364252_comment'></div>由是交道遂广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364252_comment'></div>声名益振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364252_comment'></div>朱家大侠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364252_comment'></div>滕公有然诺之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364252_comment'></div>剧孟过人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364252_comment'></div>袁盎有逢迎之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364252_comment'></div>及其从微至著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364252_comment'></div>资父事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364252_comment'></div>藉丹书之勋业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364252_comment'></div>参<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_87_1364252", 1364252, "Clauses/87/Comments/0")'>黑衣</span>之行伍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364252_comment'></div>神宫海外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364252_comment'></div>瞻镂榜于明山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364252_comment'></div>太室云端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364252_comment'></div>听仙簧于洛水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364252_comment'></div>翊驾驰道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364252_comment'></div>周庐甲观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364252_comment'></div>方当奉词出使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364252_comment'></div>万里行封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364252_comment'></div>受命忘身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364252_comment'></div>三军拜将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364252_comment'></div>岂期年岁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_98_1364252", 1364252, "Clauses/98/Comments/0")'>朝露</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364252_comment'></div>浮生过隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364252_comment'></div>汉逸人之雅操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364252_comment'></div>命也如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364252_comment'></div>鲁司寇之知言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364252_comment'></div>苗而不秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364252_comment'></div>呜乎哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364252_comment'></div>望吾子者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364252_comment'></div>空怀<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_106_1364252", 1364252, "Clauses/106/Comments/0")'>倚闾</span>之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364252_comment'></div>嗟予弟者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364252_comment'></div>独有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_108_1364252", 1364252, "Clauses/108/Comments/0")'>亡琴</span>之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364252_comment'></div>从日月于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_109_1364252", 1364252, "Clauses/109/Comments/0")'>龟谋</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364252_comment'></div>考图书于马鬣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364252_comment'></div>越以仪凤三年春二月某日甲子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364252_comment'></div>葬于某所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364252_comment'></div>悲夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364252_comment'></div>吾见其进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364252_comment'></div>由来孔李之家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364252_comment'></div>吾谓之甥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364252_comment'></div>实曰何刘之族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364252_comment'></div>阳元既殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364252_comment'></div>瞻旧宅而无成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364252_comment'></div>康伯不存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364252_comment'></div>对元言而谁与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364252_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364252_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_123_1364252'>山河带砺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364252_comment'></div>金木精灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364252_comment'></div>磊磊千丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364252_comment'></div>森森五兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364252_comment'></div>騑骖西掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364252_comment'></div>出入东明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364252_comment'></div>人寿无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364252_comment'></div>皇天不平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364252_comment'></div>碑留郭泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364252_comment'></div>挽送田横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364252_comment'></div>终寂寥于相宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364252_comment'></div>空嗟叹于佳城。</div><div id='poem_sentence_134_1364252_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_0_1364246_comment'></div>乘轮满于十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364246_comment'></div>齐景公之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1364246", 1364246, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>利用厚生</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364246_comment'></div>有马盈于千驷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364246_comment'></div>羽旄冠剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364246_comment'></div>摐金鸣玉叠其前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364246_comment'></div>苑囿池台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364246_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364246", 1364246, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>清歌妙舞</span>喧其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364246_comment'></div>崇高在于宠禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364246_comment'></div>大欲存于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1364246", 1364246, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>食货</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364246_comment'></div>义然后取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364246_comment'></div>横玉带以当仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364246_comment'></div>道不虚行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364246_comment'></div>坐盐梅而自得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364246_comment'></div>若乃时之不与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364246_comment'></div>数之不通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364246_comment'></div>贵贱任于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364246_comment'></div>穷通由于命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364246_comment'></div>左太冲之咏史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364246_comment'></div>下僚实英俊之场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364246_comment'></div>嵇叔夜之著书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364246_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1364246", 1364246, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>贱职</span>为老庄之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364246_comment'></div>虽复势力以高下相悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364246_comment'></div>尊卑以商周不敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364246_comment'></div>孔宣父中都之小宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364246_comment'></div>幽厉多谢于陪臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364246_comment'></div>陈仲弓太邱之一官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364246_comment'></div>公卿有惭于县长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364246_comment'></div>是以德成者上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364246_comment'></div>道在斯尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364246_comment'></div>陶潜则安枕北窗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364246_comment'></div>言偃则鸣弦东武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364246_comment'></div>抑扬足以仪四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364246_comment'></div>顾盼足以破三军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364246_comment'></div>代有人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364246_comment'></div>斯为盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364246_comment'></div>公讳晃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364246_comment'></div>乐安博昌人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364246_comment'></div>其后因官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364246_comment'></div>遂家蒲州之永乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364246_comment'></div>天子令德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364246_comment'></div>轩皇为诞姓之源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364246_comment'></div>诸侯计功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364246_comment'></div>薛国在宗盟之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364246_comment'></div>西京执法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364246_comment'></div>则有御史大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364246_comment'></div>东汉循良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364246_comment'></div>则有会稽都尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364246_comment'></div>任光乡里之忠厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364246_comment'></div>任隗朝臣之鲠直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364246_comment'></div>益州从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364246_comment'></div>术数知名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364246_comment'></div>临海真人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364246_comment'></div>清贞克巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364246_comment'></div>况乎东西海岱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364246_comment'></div>强齐九合之都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364246_comment'></div>表里山河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364246_comment'></div>全晋三分之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364246_comment'></div>车马雷骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_286_1364246_comment'></div>宝钗虚赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_287_1364246_comment'></div>玉树长沦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1364246_comment'></div>辅德无辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1364246_comment'></div>亲仁不亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1364246_comment'></div>百年夭枉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1364246_comment'></div>一旦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_292_1364246", 1364246, "Clauses/292/Comments/0")'>归真</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1364246_comment'></div>雷鸣之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1364246_comment'></div>长河之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1364246_comment'></div>旌旃委郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_295_1364246_comment'></div>徒御逡巡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_296_1364246_comment'></div>悲风汨起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_297_1364246_comment'></div>血下沾巾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_298_1364246_comment'></div>死而可赎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_299_1364246_comment'></div>人百其身。</div><div id='poem_sentence_300_1364246_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=679&endYear=679')">679年</a>　为弘文馆校书郎.作《从弟去盈墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷9第150页。张谱第185页言此墓志作于仪凤四年,然括注为677年,误,当为679年。）</span><div id='poem_1364250' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364250' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364250?labeling=true' target='_blank'>从弟去盈墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（679年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364250")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364250_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364250'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364250'>古者皇帝轩辕氏没。帝喾高辛氏作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364250_comment'></div>幼而徇齐。长而敦敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364250_comment'></div>则天下之人用其教者百年。忠肃恭懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364250_comment'></div>宣慈惠和。则天下之人谓之才者八子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364250_comment'></div>赤乌流而白鱼跃。有周武之兴王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364250_comment'></div>彤弓一而卢矢千。有晋文之启霸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364250_comment'></div>虽隐公逊位。哀侯失国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364250_comment'></div>而文之昭也。武之穆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364250_comment'></div>司徒为五教之官。有社稷焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364250_comment'></div>有黎人焉。丞相临万几之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364250_comment'></div>崤函鼎盛。赫奕于朱轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364250_comment'></div>河洛台阶。昭彰于白玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364250_comment'></div>积善馀庆。信而有徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364250_comment'></div>国子进士杨去盈。字流谦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364250_comment'></div>宏农华阴人也。曾祖讳初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364250_comment'></div>周大将军。隋宗正卿常州刺史顺阳公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364250_comment'></div>皇朝左光禄大夫华山郡开国公。食邑本乡二千五百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364250_comment'></div>唐虞之稷契。魏晋之裴王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364250_comment'></div>晏婴可以事百君。皋陶为之谟九德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364250_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1364250", 1364250, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>麾盖</span>兵马。人知牧伯之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364250_comment'></div>名山大川。地积公侯之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364250_comment'></div>王考讳安。伪郑王充遥授二十八将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364250_comment'></div>封鄫国公。寻谋归顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364250_comment'></div>为充所害。皇朝赠大将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364250_comment'></div>旌忠烈也。陶谦雅尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364250_comment'></div>祖逖雄心。会天子之蒙尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364250_comment'></div>见诸侯之释位。虽陈平去就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364250_comment'></div>潜怀仗剑之谋。而石勒凶残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364250_comment'></div>遂及推墙之祸。父某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364250_comment'></div>润州句容遂州长江二县令朝散大夫行邓州司马。文武兼备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364250_comment'></div>清明在躬。人无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364250_comment'></div>位不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1364250", 1364250, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>充量</span>。四方取则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364250_comment'></div>孔宣父之践中都。百里非才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364250_comment'></div>庞士元之登别驾。若夫庭生玉树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364250_comment'></div>身带金镮。有卫玠之风神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364250_comment'></div>有张良之容貌。蒋琬之讥盛允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364250_comment'></div>责在司空。陈蕃之对薛勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364250_comment'></div>志清天下。观其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1364250", 1364250, "Clauses/75/Comments/0")'>昏定晨省</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364250_comment'></div>立身扬名。怪草蔚其休徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364250_comment'></div>神鱼会其冥感。庄公独叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364250_comment'></div>闻颍叔之纯深。有道相推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364250_comment'></div>见茅容之尽礼。则闺门雍穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364250_comment'></div>以孝闻也。辅仁会友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364250_comment'></div>合志同方。晏平仲之善交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364250_comment'></div>鲍叔牙之知我。张堪死日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364250_comment'></div>妻子唯托于朱晖。刘惔生平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364250_comment'></div>风月每思于元度。则朋友之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364250_comment'></div>若兰芬也。朱穆好学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364250_comment'></div>终日忘餐。谯周<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1364250", 1364250, "Clauses/97/Comments/0")'>研精</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364250_comment'></div>欣然独笑。张华四海之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364250_comment'></div>若指诸掌。班固百家之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364250_comment'></div>无不穷究。钩深致远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364250_comment'></div>悦邱坟也。八音繁会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364250_comment'></div>五色章明。动天地而感鬼神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364250_comment'></div>序人伦而成孝敬。阳台并作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364250_comment'></div>楚襄王赐云梦之田。上林同时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364250_comment'></div>汉武帝给尚书之笔。则琼敷玉藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364250_comment'></div>未足多也。自摄齐东序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364250_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_58_1364250", 1364250, "Clauses/116/Comments/0")'>撰杖</span>西胶。唯宰我之能言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364250_comment'></div>贵颜回之有德。成如麟角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364250_comment'></div>道尊于璧水之前。翼若鸿毛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364250_comment'></div>俯拾于金门之下。方将咫尺宣室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364250_comment'></div>扈从明庭。申贾谊之忠谠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364250_comment'></div>尽扬雄之规谏。豫章七载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364250_comment'></div>擢修干而耸长条。有鸟三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364250_comment'></div>搏积风而运沧海。岂期数有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1364250", 1364250, "Clauses/131/Comments/0")'>迍否</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364250_comment'></div>天无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1364250", 1364250, "Clauses/132/Comments/0")'>皂白</span>。苗而不秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364250_comment'></div>秀而不实。盖有是夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364250_comment'></div>古人有言。没而不朽者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364250_comment'></div>此之谓也。春秋二十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364250_comment'></div>以上元三年五月二十二日。殁于京师胜业里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364250_comment'></div>呜乎哀哉。至仪凤四年十二月二日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364250_comment'></div>归葬于华阴之某原。不忘本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364250_comment'></div>山河郁郁。松柏苍苍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364250_comment'></div>骨肉闭兮归后土。魂魄游兮思故乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364250_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_75_1364250", 1364250, "Clauses/150/Comments/0")'>三荆</span>摇落。五都悲凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364250_comment'></div>痛门户之无主。悼人琴之两忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364250_comment'></div>呜乎哀哉。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364250_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_78_1364250'>高掌远蹠。浊泾清渭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364250_comment'></div>天子诸侯。司空太尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364250_comment'></div>星辰鼓舞。山泽通气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364250_comment'></div>道在者尊。德成为贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364250_comment'></div>贾家三虎。伟节最怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364250_comment'></div>荀氏八龙。慈明无双。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364250_comment'></div>剑光冲斗。璧气浮江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364250_comment'></div>据于道德。闻于家邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364250_comment'></div>子之承亲。温席扇枕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364250_comment'></div>子之友悌。同舆共寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364250_comment'></div>朝歌不入。盗泉不饮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364250_comment'></div>垂露崩云。繁纮缛锦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364250_comment'></div>明经太学。射策鸿都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364250_comment'></div>扬名天子。高揖司徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364250_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_1364250", 1364250, "Clauses/184/Comments/0")'>鳞翮</span>将运。波涛不虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364250_comment'></div>子之丧也。良可悲夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364250_comment'></div>瞻望不及。伫立以泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364250_comment'></div>唯见黄埃。心伤以摧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364250_comment'></div>踯躅兮徘徊。呜乎兮哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364250_comment'></div>长夜漫漫何时旦。魂兮魂兮归去来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364250_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_98_1364250_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=679&endYear=679')">679年6月</a>　是年六月,改年号调露.年底,秩满将改官,告病居家,作《浑天赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷1第1页。）</span><div id='poem_1364184' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364184' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364184?labeling=true' target='_blank'>浑天赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（679年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364184")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364184_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1364184'>显庆五年。炯时年十一。待制宏文馆。上元三年。始以应制举补校书郎。朝夕灵台之下。备见铜浑之象。寻返初服。卧病丘园。二十年而一徙官。斯亦拙之效也。代之言天体者。未知浑盖孰是。代之言天命者。以为祸福由人。故作浑天赋以辩之。其辞曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1364184_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364184'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364184'>客有为宣夜之学者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364184_comment'></div>喟然而言曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364184_comment'></div>旁望万里之横山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364184_comment'></div>而皆青翠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364184_comment'></div>俯察千仞之深谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364184_comment'></div>而皆黝黑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364184_comment'></div>苍苍在上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364184_comment'></div>非其正色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364184_comment'></div>远而望之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364184_comment'></div>无所至极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364184_comment'></div>日月载于元气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364184_comment'></div>所以或中而或昃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364184_comment'></div>星辰浮于太空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364184_comment'></div>所以有行而有息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364184_comment'></div>故知天常安而不动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364184_comment'></div>地极深而不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364184_comment'></div>可以为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364184", 1364184, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>观象</span>之准绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364184_comment'></div>可以作谈天之楷式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364184_comment'></div>有称周髀之术者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364184_comment'></div>冁然而笑曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364184_comment'></div>阳动而阴静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364184_comment'></div>天回而地游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364184_comment'></div>天如倚盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364184_comment'></div>地若<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1364184", 1364184, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>浮舟</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364184_comment'></div>出于卯入于酉而生昼夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364184_comment'></div>交于奎合于角而有春秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364184_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1364184", 1364184, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>天则</span>西北既倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364184_comment'></div>而三光北转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364184_comment'></div>地则东南不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364184_comment'></div>而万水东流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364184_comment'></div>比于圆首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364184_comment'></div>前临胸者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364184_comment'></div>后不能覆背。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364184_comment'></div>方于执炬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364184_comment'></div>南称明者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364184_comment'></div>北可以言幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364184_comment'></div>此天与而不取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364184_comment'></div>恶遑遑而更求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364184_comment'></div>太史公有睟其容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364184_comment'></div>乃盱衡而告曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364184_comment'></div>楚既失之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364184_comment'></div>齐亦未为得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364184_comment'></div>言宣夜者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364184_comment'></div>星辰不可以阔狭有常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364184_comment'></div>言盖天者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364184_comment'></div>漏刻不可以春秋各半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364184_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1364184", 1364184, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>周三径一</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364184_comment'></div>远近乖于辰极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364184_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1364184", 1364184, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>东井</span>南箕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364184_comment'></div>曲直殊于河汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364184_comment'></div>明入于地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364184_comment'></div>葛稚川所以有辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364184_comment'></div>日应于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364184_comment'></div>桓君山由其发难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364184_comment'></div>假苏秦之不死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364184_comment'></div>既莫知其为说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364184_comment'></div>傥隶首之重生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364184_comment'></div>亦不能成其算也。<div id='poem_sentence_59_1364184_comment'></div>原夫杳杳冥冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364184_comment'></div>天地之精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364184_comment'></div>混混沌沌。<div id='poem_sentence_73_1364184_comment'></div>一南而物死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364184_comment'></div>地之平也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364184_comment'></div>景短而多暑。<div id='poem_sentence_78_1364184_comment'></div>成其薄蚀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364184_comment'></div>众星傅月之光也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364184_comment'></div>因其波澜。<div
