class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364190_comment'></div>朝游夕处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364190_comment'></div>徘徊顾慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364190_comment'></div>叹摇落于三秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364190_comment'></div>委贞芳于十步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364190_comment'></div>伊纤茎之菲薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364190_comment'></div>荷君子之恩遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364190_comment'></div>不羡池水之芙蓉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364190_comment'></div>愿比瑶山之桂树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364190_comment'></div>岁如何其岁已秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364190_comment'></div>丛菊芳兮庭之幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364190_comment'></div>君子至止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364190_comment'></div>怅容与而淹留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364190_comment'></div>岁如何其岁将逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364190_comment'></div>丛菊芳兮庭之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364190_comment'></div>君子至止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364190_comment'></div>聊从容以卒岁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_96_1364190_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=682&endYear=682')">682年</a>　秋,高宗手诏慰问辅臣及东宫诸官,杨炯代刘仁轨、裴炎、薛元超等作谢上书《为刘少傅等谢敕书慰劳表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷5第74页。）</span><div id='poem_1364192' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364192' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364192?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为刘少傅等谢敕书慰劳表</a><span class='authorDate'>（682年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364192")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364192_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364192'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364192'>臣某等言。司马郎中王知敬至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364192_comment'></div>伏奉今月日手诏。璿玑下照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364192_comment'></div>睹天象之三光。玉检前开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364192_comment'></div>见河洛之八卦。发挥圭璧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364192_comment'></div>感召风云。不知手之舞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364192_comment'></div>足之蹈之者也。臣等稽之天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364192_comment'></div>明山辟长男之宫。步之日星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364192_comment'></div>乐府奏重光之曲。三王所以立教者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364192_comment'></div>天子为先。万国所以称贞者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364192_comment'></div>元良是寄。伏惟天皇御中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364192_comment'></div>道践平阶。对扬文武之休命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364192_comment'></div>绍述古先之大业。洛京朝韨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364192_comment'></div>义协于省方。秦地山河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364192_comment'></div>事资于监守。皇太子一物三善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364192_comment'></div>四方继明。孝以承亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364192_comment'></div>显于直城之路。明以照下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364192_comment'></div>验于长寿之街。虔奉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364192", 1364192, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>丝纶</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364192_comment'></div>躬亲政事。德刑详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364192_comment'></div>既远安而迩肃。博爱先之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364192_comment'></div>亦涂歌而里咏。固以礼成恭敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364192_comment'></div>道洽温文。知宝历之无疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364192_comment'></div>信苍生之幸甚。臣等窃循愚蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364192_comment'></div>谬荷恩私。或位联辅弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364192_comment'></div>职在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1364192", 1364192, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>台衡</span>。希少阳之末光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364192_comment'></div>自韬萤火。洽重海之馀润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364192_comment'></div>已息<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1364192", 1364192, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>牛涔</span>。不谓殊奖曲覃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364192_comment'></div>真文俯及。载之眉首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364192_comment'></div>奉以周旋。听葛天氏之歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364192_comment'></div>方惭此庆。闻有虞氏之石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364192_comment'></div>未均斯喜。但知怀璧之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364192_comment'></div>不可越乡。岂敢贪天之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364192_comment'></div>以为已力。倾诚每积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364192_comment'></div>候朱鸟于南宫。拜德无因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364192_comment'></div>限苍龙于左阙。臣无任云云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364192_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1364192_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=682&endYear=682')">682年9月</a>　九月,为宇文珽作神道碑。作品：《唐同州长史宇文公神道碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷6第91页。）</span><div id='poem_1364239' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364239' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364239?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐同州长史宇文公神道碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（682年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364239")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364239_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364239'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364239'>诸侯计功。其铭曰仲山甫式于百辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364239_comment'></div>大夫称伐。其铭曰正考甫恭于三命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364239_comment'></div>所以扬其先祖。所以示其子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364239_comment'></div>上古之初。刊于礼乐之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364239_comment'></div>中年以降。述于宗庙之碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364239_comment'></div>文质既殊。条流遂广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364239_comment'></div>山河永配。金石长存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364239_comment'></div>或旌原氏之阡。或表滕公之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364239_comment'></div>观百林之字者。孝廉之旧业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364239_comment'></div>于是乎不愆不忘。读黄鸟之词者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364239_comment'></div>文范之馀风。于是乎可久可大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364239_comment'></div>公讳珽。字叔珉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364239_comment'></div>河南洛阳人也。宇文归之远派。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364239_comment'></div>宇文翰之馀秩。龙火昼夜于钟山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364239_comment'></div>鹏云南北于溟海。自中州圯坼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364239_comment'></div>上国<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1364239", 1364239, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>崩离</span>。魏氏忘其宝图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364239_comment'></div>齐人弄其神器。则天有成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364239_comment'></div>周虽旧邦。文王以业重三分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364239_comment'></div>昭事上帝。武王以功成八百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364239_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1364239", 1364239, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>阴骘</span>下人。车书混一于域中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364239_comment'></div>子弟星罗于海内。方乎刘泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364239_comment'></div>乃天汉之懿亲。匹以曹洪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364239_comment'></div>即当涂之近属。及其隋室迁鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364239_comment'></div>唐运握符。固亦坛社仍存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364239_comment'></div>山河不替。曾祖显和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364239_comment'></div>后魏冠军将军朱衣直阁东夏州刺史车骑将军散骑常侍长广郡公。周赠使持节开府仪同三司延丹绥三州诸军事延州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364239_comment'></div>周书有传。对扬天命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364239_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1364239", 1364239, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>保乂</span>王家。霍去病初封冠军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364239_comment'></div>周亚夫始为车骑。剖符之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364239_comment'></div>任在于六条。建国之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364239_comment'></div>礼高于五等。祖神举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364239_comment'></div>使持节骠骑将军开府仪同三司京兆尹柱国大将军并潞肆石四州十二镇诸军并州总管东平郡公。赠少保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364239_comment'></div>周书有传。材优辅弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364239_comment'></div>业赞云雷。晋则羊祜仪同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364239_comment'></div>楚则若敖柱国。王章之拜京兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364239_comment'></div>天子闻其直言。郭伋之莅并州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364239_comment'></div>诸童符其恩信。考谊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364239_comment'></div>隋文皇帝挽郎。皇朝益州青城瀛州清苑二县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364239_comment'></div>钩深致远。直道正词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364239_comment'></div>不汲汲于富贵。每乾乾于日夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364239_comment'></div>广都蒋公炎。非无社稷之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364239_comment'></div>太邱陈仲弓。自有闺门之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364239_comment'></div>公庆成弧矢。气袭芝兰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364239_comment'></div>剑则赤山之精。照牵牛于北列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364239_comment'></div>鼎则黄云之宝。入天驷于东方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364239_comment'></div>资大孝而立身。蕴中和以成德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364239_comment'></div>词参变化。稽百代之阙文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364239_comment'></div>学富图书。阅三冬之旧史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364239_comment'></div>司徒袁粲。许之以栝柏豫章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364239_comment'></div>处士祢衡。目之以椅桐梓漆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364239_comment'></div>初任国子生。擢第授道王府参军兼郑州参军事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364239_comment'></div>横经太学。射策王庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364239_comment'></div>高阳才子。宣慈惠和之誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364239_comment'></div>武公新邑。济河洛颍之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364239_comment'></div>兼摄务殷。参卿位重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364239_comment'></div>王徽之任达。国士升车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364239_comment'></div>刘简之博闻。中郎寓直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364239_comment'></div>秩满。授遂州司户参军事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364239_comment'></div>天开井络。地泄江源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364239_comment'></div>财雄翕习于外区。栋宇相望于近甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364239_comment'></div>尹兴为政。知陆续于众人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364239_comment'></div>黄谠临官。识包咸于数子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364239_comment'></div>寻迁绛州翼城今。大梁星野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364239_comment'></div>少泽封圻。城故绛以深其宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364239_comment'></div>都新田以流其恶。实惟繁剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364239_comment'></div>载著循良。鲁国有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364239_comment'></div>无擅徵之事。南阳郡吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364239_comment'></div>罢休沐之娱。州府状闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364239_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_68_1364239", 1364239, "Clauses/136/Comments/0")'>乡亭</span>颂德。亦由礼让之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364239_comment'></div>绵竹于是乎作歌。风俗之夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364239_comment'></div>浚仪于是乎刊石。稍迁符玺郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364239_comment'></div>寻奉敕检校鸿胪本官如故。环济要略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364239_comment'></div>掌天子之符玺。刘熙释名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364239_comment'></div>表京师之心腹。是分麾节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364239_comment'></div>式赞王侯。国信不差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364239_comment'></div>郊迎有序。迁尚书职方员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364239_comment'></div>夏书禹贡。辨其川泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364239_comment'></div>周礼职方。明其物土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364239_comment'></div>清晨伏奏。几承<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_78_1364239", 1364239, "Clauses/157/Comments/0")'>题柱</span>之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364239_comment'></div>閒夜絜斋。惟有张灯之宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364239_comment'></div>诏除朝散大夫晋州司马。寻迁长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364239_comment'></div>平阳旧县。姑射灵山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364239_comment'></div>玉印仍存。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_82_1364239", 1364239, "Clauses/165/Comments/0")'>瑶城</span>未改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364239_comment'></div>习凿齿之逢宣武。三命而践侍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364239_comment'></div>管公明之谒冀州。四见而登别驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364239_comment'></div>诏迁同州长史。河西辐辏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364239_comment'></div>渭北膏腴。秦地之下邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364239_comment'></div>汉京之左辅。使君何以为政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364239_comment'></div>端右宜其得人。江统知贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364239_comment'></div>直言则陈留阮宣子。唐林荐善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364239_comment'></div>通理则汝南黄叔度。王祥纠合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364239_comment'></div>屈公辅之宏才。荀羡逸群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364239_comment'></div>壮冲天之劲翮。享年六十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364239_comment'></div>以永淳元年六月二十一日。终于华州之别业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364239_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。公元亨利贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364239_comment'></div>文行忠信。礼乐之君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364239_comment'></div>儒林之丈人。当在颜冉中求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364239_comment'></div>自是风尘外物。友于之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364239_comment'></div>伯淮与季江同寝。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_98_1364239", 1364239, "Clauses/197/Comments/0")'>朋从</span>之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364239_comment'></div>鲍叔与管仲推财。优游大学之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364239_comment'></div>藉甚平台之下。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_100_1364239", 1364239, "Clauses/201/Comments/0")'>辎车</span>就列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364239_comment'></div>化洽于二州。油轼当官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364239_comment'></div>政成于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_102_1364239", 1364239, "Clauses/204/Comments/0")'>半刺</span>。道尊德贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364239_comment'></div>而大位不跻。有志无时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364239_comment'></div>而天年不永。即以其年十月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364239_comment'></div>迁窆于郑县安乐乡之西源。嗣子某官等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364239_comment'></div>诗礼预闻。箕裘早学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364239_comment'></div>生则尽其养。刘殷积粟于七年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364239_comment'></div>殁则致其哀。唐颂绝浆于九日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364239_comment'></div>占白鹤。相<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_109_1364239", 1364239, "Clauses/219/Comments/0")'>青乌</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364239_comment'></div>郑伯所封。有咸林之采地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364239_comment'></div>晋侯所赂。有河外之城邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364239_comment'></div>其川渭水而玉璜。其镇华山而金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364239_comment'></div>习习旟旐。纷纷野田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364239_comment'></div>范巨卿则素车来哭。韩元良则缌麻设位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364239_comment'></div>大夫受梁鸿之命。终陪列士之坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364239_comment'></div>妻子从田豫之言。竟托神人之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364239_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364239_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_118_1364239'>国自东部。家承北平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364239_comment'></div>遂荒中县。奄有神京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364239_comment'></div>时逢日薄。运改天正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364239_comment'></div>二王之后。三代之英<span class='inlineComment2'>（其一）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364239_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_122_1364239'>惟宗惟祖。有典有则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364239_comment'></div>大魏将军。隆周柱国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364239_comment'></div>于穆显考。其仪不忒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364239_comment'></div>礼乐宣风。闺门表德<span class='inlineComment2'>（其二）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364239_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_126_1364239'>五才钟秀。百福与贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364239_comment'></div>蜀都曾子。汉代颜渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364239_comment'></div>公之广学。其积如山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364239_comment'></div>公之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_129_1364239", 1364239, "Clauses/258/Comments/0")'>大辩</span>。其流如川<span class='inlineComment2'>（其三）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364239_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_130_1364239'>亲则郕霍。地居周郑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364239_comment'></div>人物会同。歌谣鼎盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364239_comment'></div>设官分职。天子有命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364239_comment'></div>束发登朝。参卿军政<span class='inlineComment2'>（其四）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364239_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_134_1364239'>江汉之流。河汾之都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364239_comment'></div>礼优悬榻。任重前枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364239_comment'></div>六玺为贵。皇天降符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364239_comment'></div>九州为广。益地开图<span class='inlineComment2'>（其五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364239_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_138_1364239'>平阳守土。下部风俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364239_comment'></div>秦晋闾阎。山河𮜿躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364239_comment'></div>缇油之化。海沂之曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364239_comment'></div>始听鸡晨。行复骥足<span class='inlineComment2'>（其六）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364239_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_142_1364239'>龟长筮短。吉往凶来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364239_comment'></div>宾朋永诀。徒御相哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364239_comment'></div>华馆无象。元堂不开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364239_comment'></div>青龙水曲。白马车回<span class='inlineComment2'>（其七）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364239_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_146_1364239'>漠漠古墓。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_146_1364239", 1364239, "Clauses/293/Comments/0")'>槭槭</span>寒桐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364239_comment'></div>郭门之路。平林之东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364239_comment'></div>天光少日。地气多风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364239_comment'></div>凡生物而必死。唯君令始而善终<span class='inlineComment2'>（其八）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364239_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_150_1364239'></div><div id='poem_sentence_150_1364239_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=682&endYear=682')">682年10月</a>　冬,为其伯父杨德裔之妻李夫人作墓志铭。作品：《伯母东平郡夫人李氏墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷10第185页。）</span><div id='poem_1364259' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364259' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364259?labeling=true' target='_blank'>伯母东平郡夫人李氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（682年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364259")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364259_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364259'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364259'>夫人姓李氏。陇西狄道人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364259_comment'></div>自凉武昭王以后。一门三公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364259_comment'></div>为四海著族。国史家牒详之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364259_comment'></div>祖充颖。后周大将军滑州刺史流江郡公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364259_comment'></div>考元明。皇朝上仪同□济三州刺史成纪县男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364259_comment'></div>出入三朝。剖符分竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364259_comment'></div>秦陇河济之地。人到于今称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364259_comment'></div>天下士大夫。知与不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364259_comment'></div>莫不想望其风采。夫人生而纯深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364259_comment'></div>幼而恭敬。长而敦睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364259_comment'></div>成而和惠。年初及笄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364259_comment'></div>甫归于我。执箕帚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364259_comment'></div>奉舅姑。人不间于其娣姒妾媵之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364259_comment'></div>闺门之内。穆如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364259_comment'></div>故宗党推其令问。乡闾以为美谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364259_comment'></div>东平公守清白之基。逢太平之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364259_comment'></div>辟命交至。声闻于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364259_comment'></div>诏徵尚书郎。迁御史中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364259_comment'></div>出为棣曹恒常四州刺史。夫人辅佐君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364259_comment'></div>聿修内政。平旦纚笄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364259_comment'></div>则有君臣之严。沃盥馈食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364259_comment'></div>则有父子之敬。报反而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364259_comment'></div>则有兄弟之道。受期必诫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364259_comment'></div>则有朋友之信。其妇德也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364259_comment'></div>历职中外。声名藉甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364259_comment'></div>和其琴瑟。正其邦家者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364259_comment'></div>夫人与有力焉。盖常喟然而言曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364259_comment'></div>古者卿之内子。为大带命妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364259_comment'></div>成祭服社而献功。可不勖哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364259_comment'></div>可不勖哉。由是服浣濯之衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364259_comment'></div>躬纺织之事。筐筥锜釜之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364259_comment'></div>所以执其劳。蘋蘩蕴藻之菜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364259_comment'></div>所以明其德。非夫博文达礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364259_comment'></div>贞婉听从者。孰能与于此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364259_comment'></div>及公乞骸告老。退归初服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364259_comment'></div>夫人年踰耳顺。视听不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364259_comment'></div>每献岁发春。日南长至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364259_comment'></div>群从子弟称觞上寿者。动至数十百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364259_comment'></div>未尝不欢言善诱。借以温颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364259_comment'></div>侃侃焉。訚訚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364259_comment'></div>有孟母之风焉。有敬姜之诲焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364259_comment'></div>维永淳元年秋八月旁死魄。寝疾弥留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364259_comment'></div>终于华阴之望仙里。享年八十有一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364259_comment'></div>冬十一月一日丙辰。迁窆于永丰乡之平原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364259_comment'></div>从先兆也。东平公抚存怀旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364259_comment'></div>用痛悼于厥心。远近咸集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364259_comment'></div>宗亲毕会。生荣死哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364259_comment'></div>其此之谓矣。是日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364259_comment'></div>皇太子监守长安。炯忝为詹事司直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364259_comment'></div>不获展哀丧次。陪奉灵輀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364259_comment'></div>敢荐李禺之文。庶同潘岳之诔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364259_comment'></div>呜乎哀哉。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364259_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_1364259'>高岳之上。浮云翔兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364259_comment'></div>函谷之外。真气扬兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364259_comment'></div>建功北狄。讨西羌兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364259_comment'></div>受封南郑。家素昌兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364259_comment'></div>于赫祖考。为龙光兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364259_comment'></div>牧州典郡。佩银璜兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364259_comment'></div>降生淑质。秉祯祥兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364259_comment'></div>苕华菊茂。兰若芳兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364259_comment'></div>我有懿德。如圭璋兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364259_comment'></div>求之卜筮。鸣凤凰兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364259_comment'></div>君子至止。玉环锵兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364259_comment'></div>室家好合。琴瑟张兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364259_comment'></div>执其麻枲。供衣裳兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364259_comment'></div>羞其馈食。澄酒浆兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364259_comment'></div>诸姑伯娣。穆温良兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364259_comment'></div>姨姒叔妹。欢未央兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364259_comment'></div>公之出牧。守四方兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364259_comment'></div>夫人之化。德洋洋兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364259_comment'></div>公之告老。返维桑兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364259_comment'></div>闺门之内。道弥彰兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364259_comment'></div>正月上日。南至长兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364259_comment'></div>子孙欢庆。各称觞兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364259_comment'></div>宋云孟母。鲁季姜兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364259_comment'></div>匪怒伊教。由旧章兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364259_comment'></div>方期高举。登紫房兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364259_comment'></div>谁谓冥默。掩元堂兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364259_comment'></div>肃肃松槚。郁成行兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364259_comment'></div>沈沈厚穸。终不旸兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364259_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_80_1364259_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=682&endYear=682')">682年</a>　《王勃集序》约作于本年。<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷3第34页。）</span><div id='poem_1364204' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364204' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364204?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王勃集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（682年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364204")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364204_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364204'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364204'>大矣哉。文之时义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364204_comment'></div>有天文焉。察时以观其变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364204_comment'></div>有人文焉。立言以重其范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364204_comment'></div>历年滋久。递为文质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364204_comment'></div>应运以发其明。因人以通其粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364204_comment'></div>仲尼既没。游夏光洙泗之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364204_comment'></div>屈平自沈。唐宋宏汨罗之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364204_comment'></div>文儒于焉异术。词赋所以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>殊源</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364204_comment'></div>逮秦氏燔书。斯文天丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364204_comment'></div>汉皇改运。此道不还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364204_comment'></div>贾马蔚兴。已亏于雅颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364204_comment'></div>曹王<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>杰起</span>。更失于风骚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364204_comment'></div>僶俛大猷。未忝前载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364204_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>洎乎</span>潘陆奋发。孙许相因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364204_comment'></div>继之以颜谢。申之以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>江鲍</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364204_comment'></div>梁魏群材。周隋众制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364204_comment'></div>或苟求<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>虫篆</span>。未尽力于邱坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364204_comment'></div>或独徇波澜。不寻源于礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364204_comment'></div>会时沿革。循古抑扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364204_comment'></div>多守律以自全。罕非常而制物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364204_comment'></div>其有飞驰倏忽。倜傥纷纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364204_comment'></div>鼓动包四海之名。变化成一家之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364204_comment'></div>蹈前贤之未识。探先圣之不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364204_comment'></div>经籍为心。得<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>王何</span>于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/47/Comments/1")'>逸契</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364204_comment'></div>风云入思。叶张左于神交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364204_comment'></div>故能使六合殊材。并推心于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>意匠</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364204_comment'></div>八方好事。咸受气于文枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364204_comment'></div>出轨躅而骧首。驰光芒而动俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364204_comment'></div>非君之博物。孰能致于此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364204_comment'></div>君讳勃。字子安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364204_comment'></div>太原祁人也。其先出自有周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364204_comment'></div>浚启文明之裔。隐乎炎汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364204_comment'></div>宏宣高尚之风。晋室南迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364204_comment'></div>家声布于淮海。宋臣北徙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364204_comment'></div>门德胜于河汾。宏材继出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364204_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>达人</span>间峙。祖父通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364204_comment'></div>隋秀才高第。蜀郡司户书佐蜀王侍读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364204_comment'></div>大业末。退讲艺于龙门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364204_comment'></div>其卒也。门人谥之曰文中子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364204_comment'></div>闻风睹奥。起予道唯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364204_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/80/Comments/0")'>揣摩</span>三古。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/81/Comments/0")'>开阐</span>八风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364204_comment'></div>始摈落于邹韩。终激扬于荀孟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364204_comment'></div>父福畤。历任太常博士雍州司功交阯六合二县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364204_comment'></div>为齐州长史。抑惟邦彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364204_comment'></div>是曰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/88/Comments/0")'>人宗</span>。绝六艺以成能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364204_comment'></div>兼百行而为德。司马谈之晚岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364204_comment'></div>思宏授史之功。扬子云之暮年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364204_comment'></div>遂起参元之叹。君之生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364204_comment'></div>舍章是托。神何由降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364204_comment'></div>星辰奇伟之精。明何由出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364204_comment'></div>家国贤才之运。性非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_50_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/101/Comments/0")'>外奖</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364204_comment'></div>智乃自然。孝本乎未名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364204_comment'></div>人应乎初识。器业之敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364204_comment'></div>先乎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/106/Comments/0")'>就傅</span>。九岁读颜氏汉书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364204_comment'></div>撰指瑕十卷。十岁包综六经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364204_comment'></div>成乎期月。悬然天得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364204_comment'></div>自符音训。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/113/Comments/0")'>时师</span>百年之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364204_comment'></div>旬日兼之。昔人千载之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364204_comment'></div>立谈可见。居难则易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364204_comment'></div>在塞咸通。于术无所滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364204_comment'></div>于词无所假。幼有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_60_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/121/Comments/0")'>钧衡</span>之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364204_comment'></div>独负<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/122/Comments/0")'>舟航</span>之用。年十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364204_comment'></div>时誉斯归。太常伯刘公巡行风俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364204_comment'></div>见而异之曰。此神童也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364204_comment'></div>因加表荐。对策高第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364204_comment'></div>拜为朝散郎。沛王之初建国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364204_comment'></div>博选奇士。徵为侍读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364204_comment'></div>奉教撰平台钞略十篇。书就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364204_comment'></div>赐帛五十匹。先鸣楚馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364204_comment'></div>孤峙齐宫。乘忌侧目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364204_comment'></div>应刘<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/140/Comments/0")'>失步</span>。临秀不容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364204_comment'></div>寻反初服。远游江汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364204_comment'></div>登降岷峨。观精气之会昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364204_comment'></div>玩灵奇之肸蚃。考文章之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364204_comment'></div>徵造作之程。神机若助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364204_comment'></div>日新其业。西南洪笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364204_comment'></div>咸出其词。每有一文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364204_comment'></div>海内<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_77_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/154/Comments/0")'>惊瞻</span>。所制九陇县孔子庙堂碑文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364204_comment'></div>宏伟绝人。稀代为宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364204_comment'></div>正平之作。不能夺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364204_comment'></div>咸亨之初。乃参时选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364204_comment'></div>三府<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_81_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/162/Comments/0")'>交辟</span>。遇疾辞焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364204_comment'></div>友人陆季。友时为虢州司法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364204_comment'></div>盛称宏农药物。乃求补虢州参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364204_comment'></div>坐免岁馀。寻复旧职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364204_comment'></div>弃官沈迹。就养于交阯焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364204_comment'></div>长卿坐废于时。君山不合于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364204_comment'></div>岂无媒也。其惟命乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364204_comment'></div>富贵比于浮云。光阴踰于尺璧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364204_comment'></div>著撰之志。自此居多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364204_comment'></div>观览旧章。翾翔群艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364204_comment'></div>随方渗漉。于何不尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364204_comment'></div>在乎词翰。倍所用心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364204_comment'></div>尝以龙朔初载。文场<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_93_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/187/Comments/0")'>变体</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364204_comment'></div>争搆纤微。竞为雕刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364204_comment'></div>糅之金玉龙凤。乱之朱紫青黄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364204_comment'></div>影带以徇其功。假对以称其美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364204_comment'></div>骨气都尽。刚健不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364204_comment'></div>思革其弊。用光志业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364204_comment'></div>薛令公朝右文宗。托末契而推一变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364204_comment'></div>卢照邻人间才杰。览清规而辍九攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364204_comment'></div>知音与之矣。知已从之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364204_comment'></div>于是鼓舞其心。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_102_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/205/Comments/0")'>发泄</span>其用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364204_comment'></div>八纮驰骋于思绪。万代出没于毫端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364204_comment'></div>契将往而必融。防未来而先制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364204_comment'></div>动摇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_105_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/210/Comments/0")'>文律</span>。宫商有奔命之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364204_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_106_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/212/Comments/0")'>沃荡</span>词源。河海无息肩之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364204_comment'></div>以兹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_107_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/214/Comments/0")'>伟鉴</span>。取其雄伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364204_comment'></div>壮而不虚。刚而能润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364204_comment'></div>雕而不碎。按而弥坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364204_comment'></div>大则用之以时。小则施之有序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364204_comment'></div>徒纵横以取势。非鼓怒以为资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364204_comment'></div>长风一振。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_112_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/225/Comments/0")'>众萌</span>自偃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364204_comment'></div>遂使繁综浅术。无藩篱之固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364204_comment'></div>纷绘小才。失金汤之险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364204_comment'></div>积年<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_115_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/230/Comments/0")'>绮碎</span>。一朝清廓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364204_comment'></div>翰苑<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_116_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/232/Comments/0")'>豁如</span>。词林增峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364204_comment'></div>反诸宏博。君之力焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364204_comment'></div>矫枉过正。文之权也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364204_comment'></div>后进之士。翕然景慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364204_comment'></div>久倦樊笼。咸思自释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364204_comment'></div>近则面受而心服。远则言发而响应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364204_comment'></div>教之者逾于激电。传之者速于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_122_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/245/Comments/0")'>置邮</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364204_comment'></div>得其片言。而忽焉高视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364204_comment'></div>假其一气。则邈矣孤骞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364204_comment'></div>窃形骸者。既昭发于枢机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364204_comment'></div>吸精微者。亦潜附于声律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364204_comment'></div>虽雅才之变例。诚壮思之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_127_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/255/Comments/0")'>雄宗</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364204_comment'></div>妙异之徒。别为纵诞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364204_comment'></div>专求怪说。争发大言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364204_comment'></div>乾坤日月张其文。山河鬼神走其思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364204_comment'></div>长句以增其滞。客气以广其灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364204_comment'></div>已逾江南之风。渐成河朔之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364204_comment'></div>谬称相述。罕识其源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364204_comment'></div>扣纯粹之精机。未投足而先逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364204_comment'></div>览奔放之偏节。已滞心而忘返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364204_comment'></div>乃相循于跼步。岂见习于通方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364204_comment'></div>信谲不同。非墨翟之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364204_comment'></div>重增其放。岂庄周之失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364204_comment'></div>唱高罕属。既知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364204_comment'></div>以文罪我。其可得乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364204_comment'></div>君以为摛藻雕章。研几之馀事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364204_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_142_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/284/Comments/0")'>知来藏往</span>。探赜之所宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364204_comment'></div>随时以发。其唯应便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364204_comment'></div>稽古以成。其殆察微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364204_comment'></div>循紫宫于北门。幽求圣律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364204_comment'></div>访元扈于都洛。响像天人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364204_comment'></div>每览韦编。思宏大易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364204_comment'></div>周流穷乎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_148_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/296/Comments/0")'>八索</span>。变动该乎四营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364204_comment'></div>为之发挥。以成注解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364204_comment'></div>尝因夜梦。有称孔夫子而谓之曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364204_comment'></div>易有太极。子其勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364204_comment'></div>寤而循环。思过半矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364204_comment'></div>于是穷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_153_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/306/Comments/0")'>蓍蔡</span>以像告。考爻彖以情言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364204_comment'></div>既乘理而得元。亦研精而徇道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364204_comment'></div>虞仲翔之尽思。徒见三爻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364204_comment'></div>韩康伯之成功。仅踰两系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364204_comment'></div>君之所注。见光前古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364204_comment'></div>与夫发天地之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_158_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/316/Comments/0")'>秘藏</span>。知鬼神之情状者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364204_comment'></div>合其心矣。君又以幽赞神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364204_comment'></div>非杼轴于人事。经营训导。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364204_comment'></div>乃<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_161_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/322/Comments/0")'>优游</span>于圣作。于是编次论语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364204_comment'></div>各以群分。穷源造极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364204_comment'></div>为之古训。仰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_163_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/327/Comments/0")'>贯一</span>以知归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364204_comment'></div>希<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_164_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/328/Comments/0")'>体二</span>而致远。为言<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_164_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/329/Comments/0")'>式序</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364204_comment'></div>大义昭然。文中子之居龙门也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364204_comment'></div>睹隋室之将散。知吾道之未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364204_comment'></div>循<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_167_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/334/Comments/0")'>叹凤</span>之远图。宗获麟之遗制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364204_comment'></div>裁成大典。以赞孔门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364204_comment'></div>讨论汉魏。迄于晋代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364204_comment'></div>删其诏命。为百篇以续书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364204_comment'></div>甄正乐府。取其雅奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364204_comment'></div>为三百篇以续诗。又自晋太始元年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364204_comment'></div>至隋开皇九年平陈之岁。褎贬行事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364204_comment'></div>述元经以法春秋。门人薛收窃慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364204_comment'></div>同为元经之传。未就而殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364204_comment'></div>君思崇祖德。光宣奥义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364204_comment'></div>续薛氏之遗传。制诗书之众序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364204_comment'></div>包举艺文。克融前烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364204_comment'></div>陈群禀太邱之训。时不逮焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364204_comment'></div>孔伋传司寇之文。彼何功矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364204_comment'></div>诗书之序。并冠于篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364204_comment'></div>元经之传。未终其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364204_comment'></div>命不与我。有涯先谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364204_comment'></div>春秋二十八。皇唐上元三年秋八月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364204_comment'></div>不改其乐。颜氏斯殂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364204_comment'></div>养空而浮。贾生终逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364204_comment'></div>呜呼。天道何哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364204_comment'></div>所注周易。穷乎晋卦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364204_comment'></div>又注黄帝八十一难。幸就其功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364204_comment'></div>撰合论十篇。见行于代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364204_comment'></div>君平生属文。岁时不倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364204_comment'></div>缀其存者。才数百篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364204_comment'></div>嗟乎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_193_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/386/Comments/0")'>促龄</span>。材气未尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364204_comment'></div>殁而不朽。君子贵焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364204_comment'></div>兄勔及勮。磊落<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_195_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/391/Comments/0")'>词韵</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364204_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_196_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/392/Comments/0")'>铿鍧</span>风骨。皆九变之雄律也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364204_comment'></div>弟助及勋。总括<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_197_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/395/Comments/0")'>前藻</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364204_comment'></div>网罗群思。亦一时之健笔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364204_comment'></div>友爱之至。人伦所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364204_comment'></div>永言存殁。何痛如之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1364204_comment'></div>援翰纪文。咸所未忍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1364204_comment'></div>盖以投分相期。非宏词说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1364204_comment'></div>潸然<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_203_1364204", 1364204, "Clauses/406/Comments/0")'>揽涕</span>。究而序之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1364204_comment'></div>分为二十卷。具诸篇目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1364204_comment'></div>三都盛作。恨不序于生前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1364204_comment'></div>七志良书。空撰得于身后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1364204_comment'></div>神其不远。道或存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1364204_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_208_1364204_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=683&endYear=683')">683年3月</a>　在太子詹事府司直、崇文馆学士任.三月,李义琰致仕还洛,有诗以赠。作品：《送李庶子致仕还洛》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷2第31页。）</span><div id='poem_33050' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_33050' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/33050?labeling=true' "poem_allusion_33050")'>邵平瓜</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_33050_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_33050'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_33050'>此地倾城日，由来供帐华。<div id='poem_sentence_0_33050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_33050'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(235, "poem_sentence_1_33050")'>亭逢李广</span>骑，门接<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2433, "poem_sentence_1_33050")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_33050", 33050, "Clauses/3/Comments/1")'>邵平瓜</span></span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_33050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_33050'>原野<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_33050", 33050, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>烟氛</span>匝，关河<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_33050", 33050, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>游望</span>赊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_33050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_33050'>白云断岩岫，绿草覆<span class='link'
