id='poem_sentence_4_33050'>诏赐扶阳宅，人荣御史车。<div id='poem_sentence_4_33050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_33050'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_33050", 33050, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>灞池</span>一相送，流涕向烟霞。<div id='poem_sentence_5_33050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_33050'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_33050_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=683&endYear=683')">683年7月</a>　七月,为李冲寂作墓志铭。作品：《李怀州墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷9第146页。）</span><div id='poem_1364256' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364256' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364256?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李怀州墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（683年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364256")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364256_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364256'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364256'>公讳冲寂。字广德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364256_comment'></div>陇西狄道人也。左卫大将军西平王之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364256_comment'></div>荆州大都督汉阳王之子。今上之族兄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364256_comment'></div>原夫帝尧之绪。运期授于天汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364256_comment'></div>颛顼之冑。大命集于皇家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364256_comment'></div>光耀则若木十枝。波澜则长河九派。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364256_comment'></div>或中军桉部。金鼓所以节其声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364256_comment'></div>或刺史班条。冕旒所以彰其德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364256_comment'></div>信可谓玉林多宝。天族多奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364256_comment'></div>以御家邦。以藩王室者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364256_comment'></div>公山河诞庆。辰昴发祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364256_comment'></div>金多木少。孔文举之天骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364256_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1364256", 1364256, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>玉洁冰清</span>。华子鱼之神彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364256_comment'></div>南阳季恭伟。悬识宰臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364256_comment'></div>沛国赵元儒。窃知公望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364256_comment'></div>编汉皇之兄弟。列周室之邢茅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364256_comment'></div>天下称其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364256", 1364256, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>八才</span>。吾家号为千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364256_comment'></div>初任尚舍直长。稍迁城门郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364256_comment'></div>仍奉敕于宏文馆读书。掌舍诸宫城门列校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364256_comment'></div>诏诣东观。有黄香之博闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364256_comment'></div>赐其制书。有班游之广学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364256_comment'></div>寻授驾部员外郎。转金部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364256_comment'></div>又敕公为戎州道支度军粮使。天府充牣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364256_comment'></div>军储委积。振南宫之绂冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364256_comment'></div>誉表三台。历西蜀之江山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364256_comment'></div>荣高驷马。迁太府鸿胪二少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364256_comment'></div>丁艰去职。杨播之登太府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364256_comment'></div>初闻累迁之命。郑默之拜鸿胪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364256_comment'></div>遽见终丧之礼。卜子夏既祥五日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364256_comment'></div>弹不成声。孟献子加人一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364256_comment'></div>县而不乐。服阕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364256_comment'></div>历青德齐徐四州刺史。东临巨海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364256_comment'></div>西至长原。或全齐历下之军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364256_comment'></div>或大禹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1364256", 1364256, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>徐方</span>之地。任隆荆部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364256_comment'></div>陶侃八州。寄重浔阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364256_comment'></div>桓伊十部。迁宣州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364256_comment'></div>吴王旧邑。楚国先封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364256_comment'></div>江回<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1364256", 1364256, "Clauses/74/Comments/0")'>鹊尾</span>之城。山枕梅根之冶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364256_comment'></div>蜀郡无此。计吏则惟荐张堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364256_comment'></div>颍川尤多。玺书则但称黄霸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364256_comment'></div>巡察使以尤异闻。迁陕州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364256_comment'></div>观其井邑。虢仲上阳之故墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364256_comment'></div>度其川原。周公分陕之遗迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364256_comment'></div>唇齿通其列国。咽喉壮其天险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364256_comment'></div>善人为政。无待于百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364256_comment'></div>童子行谣。先符于两日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364256_comment'></div>于斯时也。天以顺动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364256_comment'></div>帝以会昌。修封禅于岱岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364256_comment'></div>作明堂于汶上。望山川而遍群神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364256_comment'></div>执玉帛而朝万国。制公检校司理常伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364256_comment'></div>文昌之省。遥接太阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364256_comment'></div>建礼之门。旁连复道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364256_comment'></div>万几匡赞。八座谋猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364256_comment'></div>既陪轩帝之巡。乃觌汉家之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364256_comment'></div>属阿孙南走。凭斗骨而为城居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364256_comment'></div>卫满东亡。界朝鲜而为役属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364256_comment'></div>乘舆乃诛后至。讨不庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364256_comment'></div>申命六事之人。以问三韩之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364256_comment'></div>制曰。师出辽左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364256_comment'></div>卿可为北道主人。检校营州都督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364256_comment'></div>石门山险。铜鼎河流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364256_comment'></div>天文则营室辨方。地象则神台镇野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364256_comment'></div>供其行李。郑国有东道之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364256_comment'></div>为我主人。常山当北州之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364256_comment'></div>辽东平。以功迁蒲州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364256_comment'></div>尧都蒲坂。舜耕历山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364256_comment'></div>昭襄王始作<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1364256", 1364256, "Clauses/132/Comments/0")'>河桥</span>。穆天子至于雷首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364256_comment'></div>汝南朕之心腹。遂拜韩崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364256_comment'></div>河东吾之股肱。时徵季布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364256_comment'></div>迁少府监。忠信为主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364256_comment'></div>杨阜齐衡。清白在官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364256_comment'></div>常林比德。又除蒲州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364256_comment'></div>诸童之逢迎郭伋。再牧并州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364256_comment'></div>百姓之愿得耿纯。复临东郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364256_comment'></div>孝敬皇帝国之储嗣。乾之长男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364256_comment'></div>四极奏于重光。二年宾于上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364256_comment'></div>崇其谥号。用黄屋于羽仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364256_comment'></div>卜其园茔。象元宫之制度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364256_comment'></div>山陵之建也。以公检校将作大匠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364256_comment'></div>游衣汉寝之外。抱剑<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_79_1364256", 1364256, "Clauses/159/Comments/0")'>桥山</span>之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364256_comment'></div>百工毕力。陈琳于是乎躬亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364256_comment'></div>诸吏怀恩。魏霸于是乎无谪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364256_comment'></div>迁银青光禄大夫。行少府监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364256_comment'></div>若夫协时月。乘天正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364256_comment'></div>秦人往事。游别馆而祈年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364256_comment'></div>汉宫旧仪。下明庭而避暑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364256_comment'></div>上幸九成宫。以公检校右领军将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364256_comment'></div>本官如故。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_87_1364256", 1364256, "Clauses/175/Comments/0")'>董司</span>戎政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364256_comment'></div>以戒不虞。七校陈其甲兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364256_comment'></div>五营桉其车服。领军之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364256_comment'></div>用文武于纪瞻。右军之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364256_comment'></div>叙勤劳于常惠。寻以公事免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364256_comment'></div>左授归州司马。楚之旧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364256_comment'></div>始得子男之田。夔之先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364256_comment'></div>裁为附庸之国。人同贾傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364256_comment'></div>路似长岑。伯鶱有声于乡里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364256_comment'></div>仲任见知于笔札。制迁中大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364256_comment'></div>行兖州都督府长史。大庭之库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364256_comment'></div>少昊之墟。上直降娄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364256_comment'></div>金精吐宿。旁瞻日观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364256_comment'></div>木德题山。别乘初迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364256_comment'></div>将宣万邦之化。佩刀终爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364256_comment'></div>徒见三公之服。以永淳元年某月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364256_comment'></div>行次唐州方城县。遇疾薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364256_comment'></div>朝廷闻而伤之。赠怀州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364256_comment'></div>公严而有礼。直而能和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364256_comment'></div>行孝立身。移忠事主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364256_comment'></div>生知者上。重之以八索九邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364256_comment'></div>道在斯尊。加之以文昭武穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364256_comment'></div>故能入登常伯。出践方州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364256_comment'></div>为六卿之仪表。发三军之号令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364256_comment'></div>列长戟于门前。罗曲旃于堂下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364256_comment'></div>子孙朝夕。玉树相辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364256_comment'></div>宾客送迎。玳簪交映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364256_comment'></div>悲夫。展禽三黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364256_comment'></div>安仁再免。奚辞棘署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364256_comment'></div>俯集桐华。惨舒则不系阴阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364256_comment'></div>喜愠则不形颜色。何嗟及矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364256_comment'></div>竟游东岱之山。无所不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364256_comment'></div>旋闭南阳之墓。二年夏五月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364256_comment'></div>葬于万年县龟川乡之平原。长子某官某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364256_comment'></div>次子某官某。箕裘必复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364256_comment'></div>花萼生光。邻人泣其悲恸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364256_comment'></div>明主忧其毁瘠。观其吊客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364256_comment'></div>不无双鹤之徵。察其成坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364256_comment'></div>自有百乌之感。森森陇树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364256_comment'></div>漠漠郊烟。右元灞而浩荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364256_comment'></div>左骊山而起伏。杜陵万家之邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364256_comment'></div>非复城池。滕公驷马之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364256_comment'></div>不知年代。其铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364256_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_130_1364256'>高阳积德。武昭馀庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364256_comment'></div>宅镐开基。封唐启圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364256_comment'></div>协和万国。平章百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364256_comment'></div>天叙诸侯。礼乐宗正<span class='inlineComment2'>（其一）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364256_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_134_1364256'>周之曲阜。汉之平陆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364256_comment'></div>地则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_135_1364256", 1364256, "Clauses/270/Comments/0")'>葭莩</span>。祥惟岳渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364256_comment'></div>乡党称善。闺庭雍穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364256_comment'></div>始拜城门。即游天禄<span class='inlineComment2'>（其二）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364256_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_138_1364256'>太微之位。益部之星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364256_comment'></div>卿则有六。四至丹青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364256_comment'></div>州则有九。八牧专城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364256_comment'></div>既践台阁。仍司甲兵<span class='inlineComment2'>（其三）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364256_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_142_1364256'>倚伏无兆。遭随有运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364256_comment'></div>贾谊从王。桓谭佐郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364256_comment'></div>自忘宠辱。曾无喜愠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364256_comment'></div>人去何归。天高不问<span class='inlineComment2'>（其四）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364256_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_146_1364256'>东都门外。长乐宫边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364256_comment'></div>白马旒旐。青乌墓田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364256_comment'></div>楸梓夹路。碑石书年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364256_comment'></div>百代之后。南阳之阡<span class='inlineComment2'>（其五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364256_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_150_1364256_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=683&endYear=683')">683年12月</a>　十二月,为李嘉作墓志铭。作品：《隰川县令李公墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷9第143页。本年十二月改元弘道,然仅一个月,又于次年改元嗣圣。）</span><div id='poem_1364253' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364253' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364253?labeling=true' target='_blank'>隰州县令李公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（683年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364253")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364253_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364253'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364253'>公讳嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364253_comment'></div>字大善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364253_comment'></div>陇西成纪人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364253_comment'></div>赵郡太守雍州大中正上开府永康公之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364253_comment'></div>幽州都督镇军大将军上柱国丹阳公之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364253_comment'></div>重华以文明允塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364253_comment'></div>谟九德于皋陶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364253_comment'></div>仲尼以恭俭温良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364253_comment'></div>翻六经于柱史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364253_comment'></div>将军李牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364253_comment'></div>人主愿其同时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364253_comment'></div>河尹李膺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364253_comment'></div>天下思其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1364253", 1364253, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>执御</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364253_comment'></div>况乎衣冠代美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364253_comment'></div>祖考家声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364253_comment'></div>占于日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364253_comment'></div>为宗周之姬姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364253_comment'></div>誓以山河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364253_comment'></div>则炎汉之刘氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364253_comment'></div>公门承将相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364253_comment'></div>地积英灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364253_comment'></div>望之俨然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364253_comment'></div>横断山而郁起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364253_comment'></div>听其言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364253_comment'></div>注悬河而不竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364253_comment'></div>玉则秦王所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364253_comment'></div>天照白虹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364253_comment'></div>剑则殷帝所传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364253_comment'></div>星浮紫气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364253_comment'></div>假使蔡中郎之博学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364253_comment'></div>郭有道之人伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364253_comment'></div>何尝不迎王粲而倒屣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364253_comment'></div>为茅容而下拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364253_comment'></div>起家为太子左千卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364253_comment'></div>以调升也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364253_comment'></div>按河图于玉版。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364253_comment'></div>震一索而为长男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364253_comment'></div>考天象于铜浑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364253_comment'></div>心前星而为太子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364253_comment'></div>直城霞绕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364253_comment'></div>曲障云平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364253_comment'></div>出入<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1364253", 1364253, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>青榜</span>之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364253_comment'></div>周旋黑衣之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364253_comment'></div>稍迁越王府户曹参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364253_comment'></div>越之建国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364253_comment'></div>地居南斗之躔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364253_comment'></div>王之受封也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364253_comment'></div>礼极东门之拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364253_comment'></div>郕霍所以隆懿亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364253_comment'></div>共和所以资明德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364253_comment'></div>一言而干楚后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364253_comment'></div>即从云梦之畋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364253_comment'></div>三见而说赵王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364253_comment'></div>仍袭上卿之印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364253_comment'></div>又迁隰州令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364253_comment'></div>川原爽垲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364253_comment'></div>风俗和平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364253_comment'></div>晋献公之嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364253_comment'></div>夷吾是邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364253_comment'></div>代恭王之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364253_comment'></div>郢容为侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364253_comment'></div>阳泉依六壁之城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364253_comment'></div>孟津合三溪之水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364253_comment'></div>公以辎车就列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364253_comment'></div>墨绶当官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364253_comment'></div>有蚕绩于郕人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364253_comment'></div>用牛刀于鲁邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364253_comment'></div>市廛无竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364253_comment'></div>不假鞭丝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364253_comment'></div>学校方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364253_comment'></div>唯闻击石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364253_comment'></div>诸侯取其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_71_1364253", 1364253, "Clauses/71/Comments/0")'>轨则</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364253_comment'></div>四海瞻其仪表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364253_comment'></div>为杜陵之男子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364253_comment'></div>谁继后曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364253_comment'></div>蔑乡里之小人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364253_comment'></div>愿辞彭泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364253_comment'></div>于是退归初服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364253_comment'></div>就养私门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364253_comment'></div>戏婴儿于阶下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364253_comment'></div>扶老生于井上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364253_comment'></div>寻丁外艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364253_comment'></div>哀毁踰制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364253_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_83_1364253", 1364253, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>加人一等</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364253_comment'></div>俯就三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364253_comment'></div>服阕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364253_comment'></div>袭封丹阳公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364253_comment'></div>勋上骑都尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364253_comment'></div>公以安车礼盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364253_comment'></div>赐杖年高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364253_comment'></div>被服先王之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364253_comment'></div>优游太平之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364253_comment'></div>左琴右书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364253_comment'></div>谋孙翼子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364253_comment'></div>居常<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_94_1364253", 1364253, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>饱德</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364253_comment'></div>不言何氏之万钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364253_comment'></div>直置当仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364253_comment'></div>岂特于公之驷马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364253_comment'></div>清风可赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364253_comment'></div>必有鸾凤相期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364253_comment'></div>白雪时游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364253_comment'></div>多以神仙见属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364253_comment'></div>义形于金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364253_comment'></div>节贯于松筠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364253_comment'></div>西山五日之朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364253_comment'></div>将化羽而生翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364253_comment'></div>北海明年之验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364253_comment'></div>便展辰而至巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364253_comment'></div>以永淳元年八月二十一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364253_comment'></div>终于京师道政里之私第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364253_comment'></div>享年七十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364253_comment'></div>呜乎哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364253_comment'></div>长子随州光化县令守节等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364253_comment'></div>哀缠吊鹤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364253_comment'></div>痛结邻人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364253_comment'></div>孝之始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364253_comment'></div>则身体发肤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364253_comment'></div>所以全其性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364253_comment'></div>孝之终也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364253_comment'></div>则衣裳棺椁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364253_comment'></div>所以成其礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364253_comment'></div>天高八万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364253_comment'></div>想京兆而何从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364253_comment'></div>地阔三阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364253_comment'></div>对佳城而有恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364253_comment'></div>越宏道二年岁次甲申正月甲申朔二十六日巳酉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364253_comment'></div>陪葬于昭陵东南之平原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364253_comment'></div>炯樗栎庸材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364253_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_128_1364253", 1364253, "Clauses/128/Comments/0")'>瓶筲</span>小器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364253_comment'></div>仰惟先友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364253_comment'></div>叨雅契于金环。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364253_comment'></div>俯逮嘉姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364253_comment'></div>荷深知于玉润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364253_comment'></div>南容有道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364253_comment'></div>仅闻将圣之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364253_comment'></div>东武建茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364253_comment'></div>俄述安仁之赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364253_comment'></div>呜乎哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364253_comment'></div>乃作铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364253_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_139_1364253'>爰初帝子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364253_comment'></div>尧之大理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364253_comment'></div>降及真人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364253_comment'></div>国之柱史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364253_comment'></div>衣冠百代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364253_comment'></div>庆灵千祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364253_comment'></div>吉兆占熊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364253_comment'></div>嘉名<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_146_1364253", 1364253, "Clauses/146/Comments/0")'>赠鲤</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364253_comment'></div>聿修厥德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364253_comment'></div>必复其始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364253_comment'></div>大孝因心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364253_comment'></div>至仁由巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364253_comment'></div>肃成门内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364253_comment'></div>章华宫里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364253_comment'></div>父任为郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364253_comment'></div>学优则仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364253_comment'></div>阳山之曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364253_comment'></div>蜀江之涘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364253_comment'></div>月旦乘凫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364253_comment'></div>田间狎雉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364253_comment'></div>其心若镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364253_comment'></div>其直如矢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364253_comment'></div>亟改炎凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364253_comment'></div>罢归桑梓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364253_comment'></div>象贤旧国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364253_comment'></div>安车暮齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364253_comment'></div>忽怆池台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364253_comment'></div>俄悲生死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364253_comment'></div>郭门一望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364253_comment'></div>郊烟四起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364253_comment'></div>夫复何言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364253_comment'></div>平生巳矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_170_1364253_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年2月</a>　二月,为王湛作神道碑。作品：《泸州都督王湛神道碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷8第116页。）</span><div id='poem_1364241' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364241' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364241?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泸川都督王湛神道碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（684年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364241")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364241_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364241'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364241'>惟汉高祖应天顺人。祭蚩尤于沛庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364241_comment'></div>斩大蛇于丰泽。则丰沛之豪杰乘于云矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364241_comment'></div>惟汉光武<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1364241", 1364241, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>龙飞凤翔</span>。举新市之八千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364241_comment'></div>破王寻之百万。则南阳之佐命动于天矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364241_comment'></div>我高祖神尧皇帝以唐侯而建国。从晋阳以起兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364241_comment'></div>协和万邦。光宅天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364241_comment'></div>则太原之衣冠有大勋矣。公讳湛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364241_comment'></div>字怀元。太原晋阳人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364241_comment'></div>十一代祖卓。晋给事中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364241_comment'></div>母常山公主。河东有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1364241", 1364241, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>汤沐邑</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364241_comment'></div>因家焉。葬于长寿县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364241_comment'></div>故乡有太原之号。皇业伊始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364241_comment'></div>公以中涓从事赐田鄠杜间。今为雍州人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364241_comment'></div>昔武王定于下人。太子宾于上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364241_comment'></div>基丰镐而开国。籍神仙以命氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364241_comment'></div>霸则司徒所让位。天子所不臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364241_comment'></div>昶则孝弟于闺门。务学于师友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364241_comment'></div>岂直横江斩将。南登建业之台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364241_comment'></div>玉食金沟。北徙邙山之宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364241_comment'></div>自兹厥后。数百年间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364241_comment'></div>国移三统。周人共推其代禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364241_comment'></div>家徙五陵。汉朝不易其冠冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364241_comment'></div>曾祖迈。后魏中书侍郎彭城王府司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364241_comment'></div>周春官大夫都督晋阳侯。祖亮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364241_comment'></div>本州主簿司水上士。隋赠信州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364241_comment'></div>太名革于东魏。天命集于西周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364241_comment'></div>宗伯所以辨其仪。林衡所以平其守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364241_comment'></div>父绰。秦孝王府掾仁寿宫监离石郡通守晋阳侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364241_comment'></div>皇朝石州刺史。逆贼刘武周攻陷郡城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364241_comment'></div>因而遇害。赠代州总管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364241_comment'></div>谥曰烈侯。礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364241_comment'></div>天造草昧。王业艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364241_comment'></div>周师才至于太原。胡兵遂入于离石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364241_comment'></div>负户而汲。不能定西戎之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364241_comment'></div>析骸而爨。不能解南楚之围。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364241_comment'></div>仁者杀身以成名。君子有死而无贰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364241_comment'></div>公承圣贤之末代。属丧乱之宏多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364241_comment'></div>天子乘舆。方靖秣陵之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364241_comment'></div>诸侯斧钺。莫救骊山之烽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364241_comment'></div>国有命而何言。邦无道而斯隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364241_comment'></div>大业之季。本州察孝廉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364241_comment'></div>非其好也。高祖乃操斗极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364241_comment'></div>拜图书。再驾临于孟津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364241_comment'></div>五星合于东井。公解衣而济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364241_comment'></div>策杖而行。郦食其之长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364241_comment'></div>逢汉祖而长揖。袁曜卿之茂才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364241_comment'></div>见曹公而不拜。从平霍邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364241_comment'></div>授紫金光禄大夫。入长安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364241_comment'></div>加左光禄大夫。历丞相相国二府典签参军事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364241_comment'></div>高祖受禅。擢为通事舍人通直散骑侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364241_comment'></div>封金水县侯。食邑七百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364241_comment'></div>稍迁虞部郎中。丁烈侯艰去职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364241_comment'></div>寻起为陇西别驾商鄜二州刺史上柱国荆州大都督府司马冀州刺史。定其封邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364241_comment'></div>誓以河山。萧相立功于万代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364241_comment'></div>留侯决策于千里。愿持一郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364241_comment'></div>洛阳之任耿纯。兼摄八州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364241_comment'></div>江都之拜陶侃。龙朔三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364241_comment'></div>迁使持节东督泸荣溱珍四州诸军事泸州刺史。江阳县地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364241_comment'></div>泸水提封。参伐下而为益州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364241_comment'></div>岐山上而为井络。尺兵再戢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364241_comment'></div>黄昌两日之歌。槃水斯来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364241_comment'></div>景伯三年之化。功成露冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364241_comment'></div>岁及悬车。叹疏广之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_1364241", 1364241, "Clauses/125/Comments/0")'>知足</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364241_comment'></div>慕祁奚之请老。乾封二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364241_comment'></div>上书乞骸骨。诏公禄赐同京官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364241_comment'></div>仍朝朔望。天子历吉日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364241_comment'></div>协灵辰。郊上元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364241_comment'></div>祀清庙。诏公行太尉事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364241_comment'></div>国之大事。摄在有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364241_comment'></div>苍璧黄琮。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_69_1364241", 1364241, "Clauses/139/Comments/0")'>六玉</span>以昭天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364241_comment'></div>路鼓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1364241", 1364241, "Clauses/140/Comments/0")'>阴竹</span>。九变而祠祖考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364241_comment'></div>名遂身退。居常待终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364241_comment'></div>山川则群望并走。星象则中台夜坼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364241_comment'></div>春秋九十有三。以咸亨三年七月十七日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364241_comment'></div>薨于京师永崇里。谥曰敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364241_comment'></div>丧事官给。赐物三百段。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364241_comment'></div>米粟三百石。葬日车服往还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364241_comment'></div>有司监护。公幼钟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_77_1364241", 1364241, "Clauses/155/Comments/0")'>偏罚</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364241_comment'></div>毁瘠过人。八岁读诗至无母何恃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364241_comment'></div>废书恸哭。呕血数升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364241_comment'></div>逮事继亲。孝闻州党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364241_comment'></div>恩深母子。比王元之事亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364241_comment'></div>梦感夫妻。等衡卿之至孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364241_comment'></div>年才一纪。有若成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364241_comment'></div>吏部薛公。见而称叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364241_comment'></div>颍川之司马德操。早知刘廙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364241_comment'></div>谯国之夏侯泰初。深叹乐毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364241_comment'></div>兵次霍邑。力战有功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364241_comment'></div>高祖嘉之。赐良马一匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364241_comment'></div>进围京城。为伏弩所中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364241_comment'></div>高祖临视。赐物三百段。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364241_comment'></div>流血及屦。未绝鼓音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364241_comment'></div>左轮朱殷。岂敢言病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364241_comment'></div>武德之始。奉使岭南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364241_comment'></div>冯盎等稽首称臣。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_94_1364241", 1364241, "Clauses/189/Comments/0")'>献琛</span>奉贽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364241_comment'></div>舍人薛卓。遇害北庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364241_comment'></div>诏公责问。单于谢罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364241_comment'></div>赐黄金五十斤。杂䌽二百段。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364241_comment'></div>南踰涨海。北渡阴山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364241_comment'></div>大中大夫去尉佗之黄屋。高车使者作匈奴之铁券。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364241_comment'></div>离石之难也。枕干而寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364241_comment'></div>见星而行。号泣不绝声者千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364241_comment'></div>水浆不入口者数日。同武陵之任袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364241_comment'></div>入搆诸羌。异河内之张武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364241_comment'></div>空持遗剑。吴远由其得铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364241_comment'></div>王裒以之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_105_1364241", 1364241, "Clauses/210/Comments/0")'>攀柏</span>。冀州境内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364241_comment'></div>旧多淫祀。褰帷按部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364241_comment'></div>申明法禁。诏书<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_107_1364241", 1364241, "Clauses/215/Comments/0")'>迁秩</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364241_comment'></div>百姓攀车。立庙生祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364241_comment'></div>树碑颂德。亦犹栾巴典郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364241_comment'></div>山鬼潜移。张禹牧州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364241_comment'></div>江涛不起。公出身六十载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364241_comment'></div>遗爱二十州。遂罢<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_112_1364241", 1364241, "Clauses/225/Comments/0")'>方岳</span>之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364241_comment'></div>仍居上台之位。始于拨乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364241_comment'></div>伊尹之辅成汤。终于太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364241_comment'></div>轩辕之得风后。然后拂衣高蹈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364241_comment'></div>躬览载籍。著遗诫十八章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364241_comment'></div>盛行于代。法文王周易之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364241_comment'></div>象尼父孝经之篇。穷性命之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364241_comment'></div>尽天人之际。庄周著论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364241_comment'></div>生也若浮。史佚立言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364241_comment'></div>殁而不朽。越文明元年二月十七日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364241_comment'></div>陪葬于献陵。礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364241_comment'></div>长子朝散大夫行扶风令遐观等。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_123_1364241", 1364241, "Clauses/247/Comments/0")'>生刍</span>一束。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364241_comment'></div>泣血三年。不踰圣人之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364241_comment'></div>能行大夫之孝。京兆载开其新阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364241_comment'></div>昆吾用昭其旧德。百年宫室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364241_comment'></div>宛在章台之东。五校军营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364241_comment'></div>依然茂陵之下。其铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364241_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_129_1364241'>昔在汤武。阿衡尚父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364241_comment'></div>下及高光。萧何邓禹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364241_comment'></div>皇天眷命。赫矣高祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364241_comment'></div>惟岳降神。克生元辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364241_comment'></div>攻城野战。张飞关羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364241_comment'></div>奇策密谋。荀彧贾诩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364241_comment'></div>始陪营卫。仍参幕府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364241_comment'></div>旌节<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_136_1364241", 1364241, "Clauses/272/Comments/0")'>龙沙</span>。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_136_1364241", 1364241, "Clauses/273/Comments/0")'>轩旗</span>象浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364241_comment'></div>出临<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_137_1364241", 1364241, "Clauses/274/Comments/0")'>方岳</span>。入调风雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364241_comment'></div>其生也荣。池台钟鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364241_comment'></div>其死也哀。陈兵复土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364241_comment'></div>孝乎惟孝。无父何怙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364241_comment'></div>刊石勒铭。永传终古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364241_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_142_1364241_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='b410cc1a5ece43cf9a03789295e0f7c8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b410cc1a5ece43cf9a03789295e0f7c8");'><span id='b410cc1a5ece43cf9a03789295e0f7c8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=685&endYear=685')">685年</a>，36岁</div><div id='b410cc1a5ece43cf9a03789295e0f7c8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=685&endYear=685')">685年2月</a>　二月,回家乡,参加伯父杨德裔葬礼并撰写墓志铭。作品：《常州刺史伯父东平杨公墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷9第138页。）</span><div id='poem_1364254' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364254' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364254?labeling=true' target='_blank'>常州刺史伯父东平杨公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（685年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364254")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364254_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364254'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364254'>杨氏之先。其来尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364254_comment'></div>在皇为皇轩。在帝为帝喾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364254_comment'></div>在王为周武。在霸为晋文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364254_comment'></div>此之谓不朽。西京为丞相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364254_comment'></div>东汉为司徒。魏室为九卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364254_comment'></div>晋朝为八座。此之谓世禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364254_comment'></div>公讳德裔。宏农华阴人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364254_comment'></div>即常州刺史华山公之元孙。左卫将军武安公之长子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364254_comment'></div>生而岐嶷。代不乏贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364254_comment'></div>事亲以孝闻。在乡党恂恂如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364254_comment'></div>始以父任为太子左千牛备身。转秀容华亭福昌雒四县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364254_comment'></div>诏封东平公。策勋上柱国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364254_comment'></div>是时也。天子仄席求贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364254_comment'></div>励精为化。以公屈临小县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364254_comment'></div>焉用牛刀。处治中别驾之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364254_comment'></div>方展其骥足耳。擢拜颍州幽州二司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364254_comment'></div>宽以济猛。严而不残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364254_comment'></div>每行县录囚徒。其所平反者十八九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364254_comment'></div>诏徵尚书郎御史中丞。謇謇谅直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364254_comment'></div>有王臣之节。寻以公事去官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364254_comment'></div>复拜饶州括州越州都督府三州长史。在会稽引陂水溉田数千顷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364254_comment'></div>人获其利。于今称之焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364254_comment'></div>迁棣曹恒常四州刺史。历政清白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364254_comment'></div>为当时所重。于是览先贤之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364254_comment'></div>知止足之分。罢归初服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364254_comment'></div>告老私庭。乃率<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1364254", 1364254, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>群从</span>子弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364254_comment'></div>营别业于宜神乡之望仙里。其制宅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364254_comment'></div>宗庙为先。厩库为次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364254_comment'></div>居室为后。喟然而言曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364254_comment'></div>古人所谓歌于斯哭于斯聚国族于斯者。吾知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364254_comment'></div>维文明元年夏四月某日。薨于正寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364254_comment'></div>春秋八十有五。呜乎哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364254_comment'></div>公简贵不交流俗。非礼不动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364254_comment'></div>非礼不行。望之俨然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364254_comment'></div>听其言也厉。博观史籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364254_comment'></div>不学书生寻章摘句而巳。至于台阁旧事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364254_comment'></div>法令科条。莫不成诵在心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364254_comment'></div>若指诸掌。几为尚书郎二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364254_comment'></div>御史中丞满岁。宰人者四县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364254_comment'></div>上佐及专城者九州。盛德形容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364254_comment'></div>被于歌咏。门生故吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364254_comment'></div>遍于天下。永淳二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364254_comment'></div>舆驾幸东都。召见公于金城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364254_comment'></div>顿访以得失。公采摭群言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364254_comment'></div>悉心以对。高宗嗟叹者良久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364254_comment'></div>赐几杖粟帛。乡里荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364254_comment'></div>一子令珍。早亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364254_comment'></div>朝夕温凊者四女。公慨然有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1364254", 1364254, "Clauses/95/Comments/0")'>丧明之痛</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364254_comment'></div>因<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1364254", 1364254, "Clauses/96/Comments/0")'>不豫</span>。弥留遗命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364254_comment'></div>以弟之子神毅为后。越垂拱元年春二月某日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364254_comment'></div>与夫人陇西李氏合葬于某原。礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364254_comment'></div>远近会葬千馀人。操笔而为诔者以百数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364254_comment'></div>呜乎哀哉。其铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364254_comment'></div>岩岩华山。峻及于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364254_comment'></div>上侵神气。下固穷泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364254_comment'></div>夫惟积德。生我大贤<span class='inlineComment2'>（其一）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364254_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_1364254'>滔滔河水。中国之纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364254_comment'></div>派别九都。经营万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364254_comment'></div>夫惟积润。生我君子<span class='inlineComment2'>（其二）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364254_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_1364254'>惟忻之城。惟华之亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364254_comment'></div>宜阳之地。益部之星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364254_comment'></div>公为其宰。不殒其名<span class='inlineComment2'>（其三）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364254_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_62_1364254'>汝阴之国。蓟门之北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364254_comment'></div>陂水朝黄。燕云夜黑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364254_comment'></div>公为其佐。日宣其德<span class='inlineComment2'>（其四）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364254_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_1364254'>入践郎官。含香<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1364254", 1364254, "Clauses/131/Comments/0")'>握兰</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364254_comment'></div>来居<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1364254", 1364254, "Clauses/132/Comments/0")'>白室</span>。直绳明笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364254_comment'></div>潘子一除。士师三黜<span class='inlineComment2'>（其五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364254_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1364254'>邑号鄱阳。山名括苍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364254_comment'></div>东南之美。吴会之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364254_comment'></div>展其骥足。实赖王祥<span class='inlineComment2'>（其六）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364254_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_71_1364254'>四州之大。是称都会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364254_comment'></div>千里之荣。即分麾盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364254_comment'></div>言旋旧国。保兹耆艾<span class='inlineComment2'>（其七）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364254_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_74_1364254'>生为贵臣。死为贵神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364254_comment'></div>阴堂是夜。古木非春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364254_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_76_1364254", 1364254, "Clauses/152/Comments/0")'>邓攸无子</span>。天道何亲<span class='inlineComment2'>（其八）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364254_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_77_1364254_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b5dfa68d3350455cac48d144e1377cd4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b5dfa68d3350455cac48d144e1377cd4");'><span id='b5dfa68d3350455cac48d144e1377cd4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年</a>，35岁</div><div id='b5dfa68d3350455cac48d144e1377cd4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年12月</a>　冬,在洛阳,致祭薛元超。作品：《祭汾阴公文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷10第172页。）</span><div id='poem_1364265' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364265' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364265?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭汾阴公文</a><span class='authorDate'>（684年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364265")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364265_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364265'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364265'>维大唐光宅之元祀太岁甲申冬十有二月戊寅朔丁亥御辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364265_comment'></div>杨炯以柔毛清酒之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364265_comment'></div>敢昭告于故中书令汾阴公之贵神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364265_comment'></div>惟公含<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364265", 1364265, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>纯德</span>而载诞兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364265_comment'></div>禀元精而秀出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364265_comment'></div>备百行而立身兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364265_comment'></div>半千年而委质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364265_comment'></div>属天地之贞观兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364265_comment'></div>逢圣人之得一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364265_comment'></div>若夔龙稷卨之寅亮舜朝兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364265_comment'></div>若萧曹魏邴之谋猷汉室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364265_comment'></div>悬大名于宇宙兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364265_comment'></div>立大勋于辅弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364265_comment'></div>如何斯人而有斯疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364265_comment'></div>曾未<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364265", 1364265, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>遐寿</span>中年殒卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364265_comment'></div>呜乎哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364265_comment'></div>若夫家传宝鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364265_comment'></div>地辟金沟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364265_comment'></div>文则属词而比事兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364265_comment'></div>学则八索而九邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364265_comment'></div>入则东藩之上相兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364265_comment'></div>出则南面之诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364265_comment'></div>唯尽善兮未善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364265_comment'></div>固虽休而勿休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364265_comment'></div>既知退而知进兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364265_comment'></div>亦能刚而能柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364265_comment'></div>大才则九功惟叙兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364265_comment'></div>大知则万物潜周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364265_comment'></div>崇德广业兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364265_comment'></div>乐天知命而不忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364265_comment'></div>呜乎哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364265_comment'></div>门馆虚兮寂寞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364265_comment'></div>岁穷阴兮摇落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364265_comment'></div>备物俨兮如存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364265_comment'></div>光灵眇兮焉托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364265_comment'></div>垂繐帷与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1364265", 1364265, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>祖帐</span>兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364265_comment'></div>罢歌台与舞阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364265_comment'></div>天子惜其毗余兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364265_comment'></div>群臣思其可作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364265_comment'></div>呜乎哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364265_comment'></div>拊循兮弱龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364265_comment'></div>叨袭兮簪缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364265_comment'></div>公夕拜之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364265_comment'></div>既<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1364265", 1364265, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>齿迹</span>于渠阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364265_comment'></div>公春华之日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364265_comment'></div>又陪游于层城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364265_comment'></div>参两宫而承顾盼兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364265_comment'></div>历二纪而洽恩荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364265_comment'></div>郭有道之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1364265", 1364265, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>青目</span>兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364265_comment'></div>蔡中郎之下迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364265_comment'></div>倏焉今古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364265_comment'></div>非复平生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364265_comment'></div>无德不报兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364265_comment'></div>愿摩顶而至足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364265_comment'></div>有生必死兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364265_comment'></div>空饮恨而吞声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364265_comment'></div>天惨惨兮气冥冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364265_comment'></div>月穷纪兮日上丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364265_comment'></div>藉白茅兮无咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364265_comment'></div>和黍稷兮非馨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364265_comment'></div>呜乎哀哉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1364265_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='62261d9157774bb094ea7dec7764f838_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=685&endYear=685')">685年</a>，36岁</div><div id='62261d9157774bb094ea7dec7764f838' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=685&endYear=685')">685年4月</a>　四月,为薛元超撰行状。作品：《中书令汾阴公薛振行状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷10第158页。）</span><div id='poem_1364260' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364260' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364260?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中书令汾阴公薛振行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（685年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364260")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364260_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364260'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364260'>高祖德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364260_comment'></div>魏给事中黄门侍郎御史中尉散骑常侍直閤辅国二将军齐州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364260_comment'></div>赠车骑将军仪同三司华州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364260_comment'></div>谥曰简懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364260_comment'></div>曾祖孝通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364260_comment'></div>魏中书黄门二侍郎银青光禄大夫散骑常侍关西道大行台右丞常山太守汾阴侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364260_comment'></div>赠车骑将军仪同三司齐郑二州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364260_comment'></div>祖道衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364260_comment'></div>齐中书黄门二侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364260_comment'></div>隋吏部内史二侍郎上开府仪同三司陵邛潘襄四州刺史襄州总管司隶大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364260_comment'></div>皇朝赠上开府临河县开国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364260_comment'></div>父收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364260_comment'></div>皇朝上开府兼陜东道大行台金部郎中天策上将军府记室参军文学馆学士上柱国汾阴县开国男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364260_comment'></div>赠定州刺史太常寺卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364260_comment'></div>谥曰献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364260_comment'></div>河东郡汾阴县薛振年六十二字元超状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364260_comment'></div>昔者唐尧之协和万邦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364260_comment'></div>有若四岳之敬顺昊天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364260_comment'></div>历象日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364260_comment'></div>虞舜之慎徽五典也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364260_comment'></div>有若八元之忠肃恭懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364260_comment'></div>宣慈惠和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364260_comment'></div>夏禹之分别九州也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364260_comment'></div>有若咎繇之谟明弼谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364260_comment'></div>允迪厥德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364260_comment'></div>殷汤之南征北怨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364260_comment'></div>有若伊尹之格于皇天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364260_comment'></div>姬文之受命作周也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364260_comment'></div>有若虢叔之闻于上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364260_comment'></div>自唐虞而列考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364260_comment'></div>及秦汉而无讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364260_comment'></div>元首必藉于股肱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364260_comment'></div>方隆太平之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364260_comment'></div>贤者必待于明主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364260_comment'></div>克致崇高之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364260_comment'></div>若夫骖驾六龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364260_comment'></div>驱驰七圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364260_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1364260", 1364260, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>斟酌</span>元气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364260_comment'></div>财成天道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364260_comment'></div>其惟圣人乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364260_comment'></div>宏阐大猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364260_comment'></div>发挥神化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364260_comment'></div>匡正八极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364260_comment'></div>阜成兆人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364260_comment'></div>其惟良宰乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364260_comment'></div>我大唐之建国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364260_comment'></div>粤若神尧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364260_comment'></div>明扬侧陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364260_comment'></div>文王叶于朕卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364260_comment'></div>迎太公于渭水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364260_comment'></div>高宗求于朕梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364260_comment'></div>得<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_51_1364260", 1364260, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>良弼</span>于傅岩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364260_comment'></div>若岁大旱以为霖雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364260_comment'></div>若济巨川以为舟楫者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364260_comment'></div>公含天地之间气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364260_comment'></div>依日月之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_55_1364260", 1364260, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>末光</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364260_comment'></div>能备九德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364260_comment'></div>兼资百行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364260_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_58_1364260", 1364260, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>探赜索隐</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364260_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_59_1364260", 1364260, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>极深研几</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364260_comment'></div>龆龀之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364260_comment'></div>羞言霸道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364260_comment'></div>词赋之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364260_comment'></div>巳成王佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364260_comment'></div>年六岁袭爵汾阴男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364260_comment'></div>十一太宗召见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364260_comment'></div>敕宏文馆读书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364260_comment'></div>十六为神尧皇帝挽郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364260_comment'></div>十九尚和静县主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364260_comment'></div>高宗升储之日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364260_comment'></div>敕公为太子通事舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364260_comment'></div>二十二除太子舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364260_comment'></div>高宗践位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364260_comment'></div>诏迁朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364260_comment'></div>守给事中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364260_comment'></div>年二十六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364260_comment'></div>寻拜中书舍人宏文馆学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364260_comment'></div>三十二丁太夫人忧去职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364260_comment'></div>起为黄门侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364260_comment'></div>固辞不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364260_comment'></div>修东殿新书毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364260_comment'></div>进爵为侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364260_comment'></div>公毁瘠过礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364260_comment'></div>多不视事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364260_comment'></div>出为饶州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364260_comment'></div>上梦公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364260_comment'></div>徵为右成务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364260_comment'></div>四十复为东台侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364260_comment'></div>是岁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364260_comment'></div>放李义府于邛笮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364260_comment'></div>旧制流人禁乘马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364260_comment'></div>公为之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364260_comment'></div>左迁简州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364260_comment'></div>岁馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364260_comment'></div>上官仪伏诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364260_comment'></div>坐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_95_1364260", 1364260, "Clauses/95/Comments/0")'>词翰</span>往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364260_comment'></div>徙居越巂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364260_comment'></div>五十三赦还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364260_comment'></div>拜正谏大夫。<div id='poem_sentence_100_1364260_comment'></div>五十九迁中书令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364260_comment'></div>车驾幸洛阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364260_comment'></div>诏公兼户部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364260_comment'></div>与皇太子居守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364260_comment'></div>俄以风疾不视事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364260_comment'></div>高宗崩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364260_comment'></div>舆疾往成都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364260_comment'></div>抗表辞位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364260_comment'></div>至于再至于三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364260_comment'></div>诏加金紫光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364260_comment'></div>仍听致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364260_comment'></div>呜乎哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364260_comment'></div>公地藉膏腴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364260_comment'></div>姻连戚里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364260_comment'></div>鼎湖长往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364260_comment'></div>拜卿子而为郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364260_comment'></div>金榜洞开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364260_comment'></div>徵列侯而尚主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364260_comment'></div>遂乃弹冠筮仕。<div id='poem_sentence_125_1364260_comment'></div>居外台者两郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364260_comment'></div>四迁门下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364260_comment'></div>二入中书。<div id='poem_sentence_130_1364260_comment'></div>盐梅我宝鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364260_comment'></div>梁栋我宸极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364260_comment'></div>理百官而察万人。<div id='poem_sentence_136_1364260_comment'></div>萧何曹参。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364260_comment'></div>谋猷汉室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364260_comment'></div>未有一心事主四十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364260_comment'></div>参两宫而出入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364260_comment'></div>历三台而陟降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364260_comment'></div>合其道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364260_comment'></div>大壑纵其鲲鹏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364260_comment'></div>遇其时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364260_comment'></div>名山出其云雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364260_comment'></div>功成辅弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364260_comment'></div>德迈几深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364260_comment'></div>星象不愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364260_comment'></div>方践中台之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364260_comment'></div>山川并走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364260_comment'></div>竟游东岱之魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364260_comment'></div>天不慭遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364260_comment'></div>民将安仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364260_comment'></div>越翼日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364260_comment'></div>诏赠光禄大夫使持节都督秦成武渭四州诸军事秦州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364260_comment'></div>馀如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364260_comment'></div>赐物四百段。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364260_comment'></div>米粟四百石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364260_comment'></div><span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364260_comment'></div>司宾卿监护。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364260_comment'></div>玺书吊祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364260_comment'></div>杂物百段。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364260_comment'></div>又诏陪葬乾陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364260_comment'></div>依故事也。<div id='poem_sentence_168_1364260_comment'></div>至天王狩河阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364260_comment'></div>乃废书而叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364260_comment'></div>周朝岂无良相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364260_comment'></div>何得以臣召君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364260_comment'></div>文汪异焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364260_comment'></div>神尧皇帝婕妤河东郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364260_comment'></div>公之姑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364260_comment'></div>每侍高祖<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_176_1364260", 1364260, "Clauses/176/Comments/0")'>词翰</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364260_comment'></div>高祖尝顾曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364260_comment'></div>不见婕妤侄数日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364260_comment'></div>便谓社稷不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364260_comment'></div>其见重如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364260_comment'></div>上幸温泉射猛兽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364260_comment'></div>公奏疏极谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364260_comment'></div>上深纳焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364260_comment'></div>后因闲居谓公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364260_comment'></div>我昔在春宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364260_comment'></div>与卿俱少壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364260_comment'></div>光阴倏忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364260_comment'></div>已三十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364260_comment'></div>往日贤臣良将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364260_comment'></div>索然俱尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364260_comment'></div>我与卿白首相见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364260_comment'></div>卿历观书传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364260_comment'></div>君臣共终白首者几人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364260_comment'></div>我观卿大怜我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364260_comment'></div>我亦记卿深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364260_comment'></div>公呜咽稽首谢曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364260_comment'></div>先臣早参麾盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364260_comment'></div>文皇委之以心膂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364260_comment'></div>臣又多幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364260_comment'></div>天皇任之以股肱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1364260_comment'></div>誓期杀身报国。<div id='poem_sentence_203_1364260_comment'></div>养生卫寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1364260_comment'></div>则天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1364260_comment'></div>赐金二百镒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1364260_comment'></div>公有事君之节也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1364260_comment'></div>不亦忠乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1364260_comment'></div>每读孝子忠臣传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1364260_comment'></div>未尝不慷慨流涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1364260_comment'></div>以为帝舜非孝子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1364260_comment'></div>朱云非忠臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1364260_comment'></div>客有讥之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1364260_comment'></div>公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1364260_comment'></div>宁有扬君父之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1364260_comment'></div>朕遂不识卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1364260_comment'></div>卿事朕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1364260_comment'></div>君父一致。<div id='poem_sentence_248_1364260_comment'></div>上大悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1364260_comment'></div>百官舞蹈称万岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1364260_comment'></div>赐杂物百段。<div 1364260, "Clauses/288/Comments/0")'>神通</span>之鉴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1364260_comment'></div>不亦明乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1364260_comment'></div>仪表魁杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1364260_comment'></div>鬓眉若画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1364260_comment'></div>身长七尺四寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1364260_comment'></div>望之俨然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1364260_comment'></div>喜愠不形于色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1364260_comment'></div>虽至于近习左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_295_1364260_comment'></div>胥徒仆妾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_296_1364260_comment'></div>莫不待之以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_297_1364260_comment'></div>公有行已之方也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_298_1364260_comment'></div>不亦恭乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_299_1364260_comment'></div>在饶州六年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1364260_comment'></div>以仁明驭下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1364260_comment'></div>鄱阳北冈上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1364260_comment'></div>忽生芝草一株。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1364260_comment'></div>郡人以为善政所感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_304_1364260_comment'></div>共起一舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1364260_comment'></div>号曰芝亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1364260_comment'></div>因立碑颂德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1364260_comment'></div>公有驭人之术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1364260_comment'></div>不亦惠乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1364260_comment'></div>在邛都十馀载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_310_1364260_comment'></div>沈研易象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1364260_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_312_1364260", 1364260, "Clauses/312/Comments/0")'>韦编三绝</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_312_1364260_comment'></div>赋诗纵酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1364260_comment'></div>以乐当年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1364260_comment'></div>有醉后集三卷行于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_315_1364260_comment'></div>公有安和之德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_316_1364260_comment'></div>不亦康乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_317_1364260_comment'></div>上初览万几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_318_1364260_comment'></div>公上疏论社稷安危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_319_1364260_comment'></div>君臣得失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_320_1364260_comment'></div>上大惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_321_1364260_comment'></div>即日召见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_322_1364260_comment'></div>不觉膝之前席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_323_1364260_comment'></div>叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_324_1364260_comment'></div>览卿疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_325_1364260_comment'></div>若暗室而照天光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_326_1364260_comment'></div>临明镜而睹万象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_327_1364260_comment'></div>此后宠遇日隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_328_1364260_comment'></div>每军国大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_329_1364260_comment'></div>必参谋帷幄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_330_1364260_comment'></div>在中书独掌机务者五年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_331_1364260_comment'></div>出纳帝命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_332_1364260_comment'></div>口占数百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_333_1364260_comment'></div>上曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_334_1364260_comment'></div>使卿长在中书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_335_1364260_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_336_1364260", 1364260, "Clauses/336/Comments/0")'>一夔足</span>矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_336_1364260_comment'></div>大驾东巡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_337_1364260_comment'></div>诏公骖乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_338_1364260_comment'></div>上曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_339_1364260_comment'></div>朕之留卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_340_1364260_comment'></div>若去一目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_341_1364260_comment'></div>若断一臂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_342_1364260_comment'></div>关西事重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_343_1364260_comment'></div>一以委卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_344_1364260_comment'></div>因赐物百段。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_345_1364260_comment'></div>公有社稷之勋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_346_1364260_comment'></div>不亦重乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_347_1364260_comment'></div>若夫有官功者赐其官族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_348_1364260_comment'></div>有大行者受其大名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_349_1364260_comment'></div>公叔列国之陪臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_350_1364260_comment'></div>犹安社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_351_1364260_comment'></div>黔娄匹夫之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_352_1364260", 1364260, "Clauses/352/Comments/0")'>介节</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_352_1364260_comment'></div>不忘仁义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_353_1364260_comment'></div>古今以为<span
