class='inline' id='poem_sentence_355_1364260_comment'></div>况乎辅佐明主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_356_1364260_comment'></div>宁济天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_357_1364260_comment'></div>生死无二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_358_1364260_comment'></div>始终若一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_359_1364260_comment'></div>业高于六相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_360_1364260_comment'></div>道贯于五臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_361_1364260_comment'></div>其生也荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_362_1364260_comment'></div>同心比于周召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_363_1364260_comment'></div>其死也哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_364_1364260_comment'></div>陪葬均于卫霍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_365_1364260_comment'></div>岂使易名之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_366_1364260_comment'></div>不及于会同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_367_1364260_comment'></div>赐谥之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_368_1364260_comment'></div>不传于终古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_369_1364260_comment'></div>门生故吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_370_1364260_comment'></div>愿述德音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_371_1364260_comment'></div>博士礼官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_372_1364260_comment'></div>伫闻清议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_373_1364260_comment'></div>是则钟繇之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_374_1364260_comment'></div>降于皇魏之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_375_1364260_comment'></div>王导之疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_376_1364260_comment'></div>寝于中兴之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_377_1364260_comment'></div>谨状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_378_1364260_comment'></div>垂拱元年四月四日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_379_1364260_comment'></div>故中书令汾阳公府功曹姓名谨状文昌台考功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_380_1364260_comment'></div>窃闻生为贵臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_381_1364260_comment'></div>车服昭其令德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_382_1364260_comment'></div>死而不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_383_1364260_comment'></div>谥号光其大名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_384_1364260_comment'></div>今谨桉故府主中书令汾阴公赠秦州都督薛元超。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_385_1364260_comment'></div>以王佐之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_386_1364260_comment'></div>逢太平之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_387_1364260_comment'></div>抚绥万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_388_1364260_comment'></div>康济兆人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_389_1364260_comment'></div>力牧辅轩皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_390_1364260_comment'></div>未为尽善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_391_1364260_comment'></div>皋陶佐大禹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_392_1364260_comment'></div>犹有惭德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_393_1364260_comment'></div>名遂身退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_394_1364260_comment'></div>生荣死哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_395_1364260_comment'></div>羽父之请鲁君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_396_1364260_comment'></div>抑惟旧典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_397_1364260_comment'></div>卫侯之谥文子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_398_1364260_comment'></div>庶几前列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_399_1364260_comment'></div>谨上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_400_1364260_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=688&endYear=688')">688年12月</a>　十二月,宴于皇甫氏宅,作文以记。作品：《宴皇甫兵曹宅诗序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷3第47页。）</span><div id='poem_1364201' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364201' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364201?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宴皇甫兵曹宅诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364201")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364201_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364201'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364201'>皇甫君冠冕于安定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364201_comment'></div>李校书羽仪于陇西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364201_comment'></div>岑正字<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1364201", 1364201, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>明目</span>于汉南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364201_comment'></div>石宫坊抵掌于河朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364201_comment'></div>高侯邦之司直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364201_comment'></div>下走齐之滥吹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364201_comment'></div>若夫风云龙虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364201_comment'></div>水火阴阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364201_comment'></div>隔千里而应之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364201_comment'></div>莫不潜契于同声矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364201_comment'></div>圣明千载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364201_comment'></div>区宇一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364201_comment'></div>掩八纮以得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364201_comment'></div>莫不高会于中京矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364201_comment'></div>是日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364201_comment'></div>河图适至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364201_comment'></div>海鲸初死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364201_comment'></div>五岳四渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364201_comment'></div>汉皇帝崇其望祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364201_comment'></div>一日三朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364201_comment'></div>周天子展其庄敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364201_comment'></div>君臣庆色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364201_comment'></div>朝野欢心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364201_comment'></div>元宴先生开甲第而留宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364201_comment'></div>二三君子赴龙门而广宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364201_comment'></div>阴云已墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364201_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1364201", 1364201, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>肃气</span>弥高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364201_comment'></div>霜寒万里之园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364201_comment'></div>冰纳千金之水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364201_comment'></div>面郊后市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364201_comment'></div>即为潘岳之居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364201_comment'></div>累代通家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364201_comment'></div>咸言李膺之客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364201_comment'></div>百年何计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364201_comment'></div>相知在于我心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364201_comment'></div>四海何求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364201_comment'></div>为乐止于名教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364201_comment'></div>抽毫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1364201", 1364201, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>进牍</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364201_comment'></div>皆请赋诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364201_comment'></div>日暮途远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364201_comment'></div>聊裁序引。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1364201_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=689&endYear=689')">689年</a>　秋,在洛阳,向武后献老人星赋。作品：《老人星赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷1第11页。）</span><div id='poem_1364191' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364191' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364191?labeling=true' target='_blank'>老人星赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（689年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364191")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364191_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364191'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364191'>赫赫宗周。皇天降休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364191_comment'></div>丽哉神圣。皇天降命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364191_comment'></div>开纲布网。发号施令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364191_comment'></div>河出图兮五云集。天垂象兮三光映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364191_comment'></div>南极之庭。老人之星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364191_comment'></div>煜煜爚爚。煌煌荧荧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364191_comment'></div>秋分之旦见乎丙。春分之夕入乎丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364191_comment'></div>配神山之呼万岁。符德水之兆千龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364191_comment'></div>晃如金粟。粲若银烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364191_comment'></div>比秋草之一萤。状荆山之片玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364191_comment'></div>浑浑熊熊。悬紫贝于河宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364191_comment'></div>奕奕炜炜。曜明珠于汉水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364191_comment'></div>其光也如丹。其大也如李。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364191_comment'></div>稽元命之攸述。按星经之所纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364191_comment'></div>见则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364191", 1364191, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>化平</span>主昌。明则天下多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364191_comment'></div>经始灵台。嵯峨崔嵬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364191_comment'></div>星则唐都讲艺。气则王朔呈材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364191_comment'></div>昼观云物。夜察<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364191", 1364191, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>昭回</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364191_comment'></div>睹南郊之炳耀。欣北极之康哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364191_comment'></div>三公辅弼。庶官文武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364191_comment'></div>献仙寿兮祝尧。奏昌言兮拜禹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364191_comment'></div>瞻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1364191", 1364191, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>太霄</span>而踊跃。伏前庭而俯偻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364191_comment'></div>万人于是和歌。百兽于焉率舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364191_comment'></div>穆穆神皇。受天之祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364191_comment'></div>邈矣台州之北。窅然汾水之阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364191_comment'></div>贞明也者。日月同光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364191_comment'></div>贞观也者。天地为常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364191_comment'></div>有混成之独立。运元气之茫茫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364191_comment'></div>若夫大虹流渚。金天当宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364191_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1364191", 1364191, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>大电</span>绕枢。轩辕受图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364191_comment'></div>殷馗则黄星见楚。雷焕则紫气临吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364191_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1364191", 1364191, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>青方</span>半月。东井联珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364191_comment'></div>辰极之齐七政。泰阶之平六符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364191_comment'></div>虽前皇之盛德。又何以加于此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364191_comment'></div>至若甘露溢。醴泉出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364191_comment'></div>蓂荚生。嘉禾实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364191_comment'></div>凤凰丹彩。驺虞白质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364191_comment'></div>南海无波。东风入律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364191_comment'></div>比夫皇穹之锡寿。何足以谈其万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364191_comment'></div>圣上犹复招列仙。择群贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364191_comment'></div>日慎一日。元之又元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364191_comment'></div>兵戈不起。至德承天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364191_comment'></div>臣炯作颂。皇家万年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364191_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1364191_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=690&endYear=690')">690年</a>　春,与宋之问一同分直设于洛阳的习艺馆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=691&endYear=691')">691年</a>　仍任教于习艺馆.为成知礼作神道碑。作品：《唐赠荆州刺史成公神道碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷7第103页。）</span><div id='poem_1364243' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364243' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364243?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐赠荆州刺史成公神道碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（691年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364243")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364243_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364243'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364243'>成氏之先。有周之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364243_comment'></div>姬文受命。三十八王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364243_comment'></div>郕伯象贤。二十一代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364243_comment'></div>汉之少府。国家维城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364243_comment'></div>晋之广杨。王室藩屏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364243_comment'></div>公讳知礼。其先上谷人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364243_comment'></div>子孙避地徙于某。曾祖休宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364243_comment'></div>后魏汾州刺史。齐特进左右卫大将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364243_comment'></div>宇文朝江州刺史。隋成阳郡公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364243_comment'></div>谥曰武。勋格皇天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364243_comment'></div>泽充区域。该备宠荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364243_comment'></div>兼包<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1364243", 1364243, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>命赐</span>。祖少遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364243_comment'></div>北齐民曹郎中。宇文朝地官上士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364243_comment'></div>袭成阳公。建国之属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364243_comment'></div>以训五品。以亲百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364243_comment'></div>父绰。隋金紫光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364243_comment'></div>唐深州刺史上柱国。天子大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364243_comment'></div>金章紫绶。天王使者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364243_comment'></div>皂盖朱轮。公诞保灵和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364243_comment'></div>受兹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1364243", 1364243, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>介福</span>。讲之以学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364243_comment'></div>合之以和。纯粹以积其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364243_comment'></div>文明以宣其外。出于口者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364243_comment'></div>必是先王之言。萌于心者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364243_comment'></div>莫非君子之德。戒慎乎其所不睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364243_comment'></div>恐惧乎其所不闻。时止时行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364243_comment'></div>左宫右徵。在朝济济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364243_comment'></div>在家雍雍。祇服宏业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364243_comment'></div>克丕堂构。袭成阳公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364243_comment'></div>历箕州平城洛州邯郸二县令。武乡里闬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364243_comment'></div>榆社堤封。公宰平城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364243_comment'></div>日宣三德。悲歌相聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364243_comment'></div>袨服成群。公宰邯郸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364243_comment'></div>雷震百里。仪刑嘉诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364243_comment'></div>范乎人伦。令问广誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364243_comment'></div>塞乎天壤。将蹈九列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364243_comment'></div>平三阶。岂意太和交薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364243_comment'></div>而天道<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1364243", 1364243, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>难谌</span>。降年不永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364243_comment'></div>春秋若干。以某年月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364243_comment'></div>终于某所。夫人宜城县主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364243_comment'></div>圣神皇帝之堂姊。王姬外馆之长女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364243_comment'></div>夫人道峻于闺房。名辉于邦国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364243_comment'></div>我大周叙洪范。作武成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364243_comment'></div>大赉而万姓悦。垂拱而天下理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364243_comment'></div>法号惟旧。制赠荆州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364243_comment'></div>生则唐尧不用。没则周武追封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364243_comment'></div>为龙为光。有始有卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364243_comment'></div>立名于后。以显其亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364243_comment'></div>反葬于周。不忘其本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364243_comment'></div>以某年月日。归葬于某原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364243_comment'></div>碣石恒山。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1364243", 1364243, "Clauses/99/Comments/0")'>燕南赵北</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364243_comment'></div>礼仪光被。宗族相临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364243_comment'></div>大夫吊桓子之丧。天子归惠公之赗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364243_comment'></div>蘧瑗之葬。不害良田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364243_comment'></div>孔邱之茔。不生荆棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364243_comment'></div>长子司卫少卿兼检校魏州刺史大辨中子左鹰扬将军大方少子朝议大夫行司汉主簿大琬等。门承四代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364243_comment'></div>德盛三贤。有终身之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364243_comment'></div>尽生人之本。玺册裒赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364243_comment'></div>宜宣无穷。景钟勒铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364243_comment'></div>若古有训。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364243_comment'></div>其铭曰。神岳之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364243_comment'></div>大川之精。如山之峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364243_comment'></div>如流之清。行之斯立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364243_comment'></div>言之斯成。登车发耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364243_comment'></div>在邦有声。传于旧国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364243_comment'></div>旧国惟平。宰于二县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364243_comment'></div>二县惟宁。余闻旧说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364243_comment'></div>天鉴孔明。谁谓灵诞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364243_comment'></div>丧落淑贞。永锡不匮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364243_comment'></div>克扬其名。册书光宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364243_comment'></div>没有馀荣。系曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364243_comment'></div>列星垂象兮炳天光。白露为霜兮沾人裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364243_comment'></div>彼苍天兮歼我良。列星垂象兮炳天晖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364243_comment'></div>白露为霜兮沾人衣。九原可作兮吾与归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364243_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_73_1364243_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=691&endYear=691')">691年</a>　秋,宋之问在陆浑山庄,有诗赠炯。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=692&endYear=692')">692年2月</a>　春,仍值习艺馆.二月,作《杜袁州墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷9第141页。本年四月,改元如意.九月,改元长寿.前之纪年,本应署天授三年,因张谱未记,故仍之。）</span><div id='poem_1364255' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364255' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364255?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杜袁州墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（692年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364255")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364255_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364255'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364255'>公讳某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364255_comment'></div>字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364255_comment'></div>京兆杜陵人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364255_comment'></div>高辛之抚教万方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364255_comment'></div>尧帝之平章百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364255_comment'></div>传称圣人之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364255_comment'></div>易曰积善之家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364255_comment'></div>在夏为御龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364255_comment'></div>在周为唐杜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364255_comment'></div>三王以降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364255_comment'></div>百代可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364255_comment'></div>车服出于南阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364255_comment'></div>衣冠袭于京兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364255_comment'></div>曾祖荣业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364255_comment'></div>后魏秦州别驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364255_comment'></div>祖良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364255_comment'></div>宇文朝复州长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364255_comment'></div>父举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364255_comment'></div>唐易州司兵参军事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364255_comment'></div>事端履道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364255_comment'></div>操矢安贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364255_comment'></div>厚于天爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364255_comment'></div>薄于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1364255", 1364255, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>人位</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364255_comment'></div>阙里之庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364255_comment'></div>学夫诗礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364255_comment'></div>太邱之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364255_comment'></div>执其羔雁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364255_comment'></div>公孝慈而敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364255_comment'></div>威庄而安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364255_comment'></div>狎贯义方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364255_comment'></div>周览典籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364255_comment'></div>服其服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364255_comment'></div>则文之以君子之容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364255_comment'></div>遂其辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364255_comment'></div>则实之以君子之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364255_comment'></div>起家左翊卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364255_comment'></div>选授贝州司仓参军事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364255_comment'></div>出自中禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364255_comment'></div>在于外台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364255_comment'></div>谨其盖藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364255_comment'></div>实其仓庾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364255_comment'></div>寻迁蓬州咸安许州长社洛州洛阳三县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364255_comment'></div>地方百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364255_comment'></div>官历三城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364255_comment'></div>言非法度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364255_comment'></div>不出于口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364255_comment'></div>行非公道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364255_comment'></div>不萌于心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364255_comment'></div>令不肃而威宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364255_comment'></div>教不舒而德洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364255_comment'></div>转虢州司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364255_comment'></div>制授朝散大夫婺州司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364255_comment'></div>又迁苏州长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364255_comment'></div>加中散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364255_comment'></div>鸾凤不栖于枳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364255_comment'></div>燕雀不集于梧桐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364255_comment'></div>宜得其材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364255_comment'></div>非公莫可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364255_comment'></div>我大周诞受万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364255_comment'></div>宠绥四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364255_comment'></div>建官惟贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364255_comment'></div>垂拱而理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364255_comment'></div>乃命公为朝议大夫使持节袁州诸军事守袁州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364255_comment'></div>天王之使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364255_comment'></div>列国之君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364255_comment'></div>发其德音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364255_comment'></div>而劝不用赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364255_comment'></div>正其颜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364255_comment'></div>而禁不用刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364255_comment'></div>德成而位尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364255_comment'></div>名遂而身退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364255_comment'></div>乞骸告老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364255_comment'></div>谢病言归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364255_comment'></div>以某年月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364255_comment'></div>终于淮海之馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364255_comment'></div>春秋七十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364255_comment'></div>呜乎哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364255_comment'></div>夫人太原王氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364255_comment'></div>魏骠骑大将军新昌公平之曾孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364255_comment'></div>唐蜀王府典军上柱国志隆之女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364255_comment'></div>纂承洪烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364255_comment'></div>嗣续徽音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364255_comment'></div>中外柔嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364255_comment'></div>小大怀睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364255_comment'></div>夫人之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364255_comment'></div>国风美于鹊巢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364255_comment'></div>宝剑之沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364255_comment'></div>夜气冲于牛斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364255_comment'></div>享年四十八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364255_comment'></div>呜乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364255_comment'></div>咸亨二年某月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364255_comment'></div>终于长社之官第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364255_comment'></div>维天授三年春二月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364255_comment'></div>合祔杜陵之平原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364255_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364255_comment'></div>王人吊祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364255_comment'></div>仪仗官给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364255_comment'></div>长子某官等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364255_comment'></div>毁形于骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364255_comment'></div>痛贯于心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364255_comment'></div>父母哀哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364255_comment'></div>昊天莫报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364255_comment'></div>佳城郁郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364255_comment'></div>白日何年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364255_comment'></div>愿述馀风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364255_comment'></div>式铭幽壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364255_comment'></div>其铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364255_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_107_1364255'>凤凰鸣矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364255_comment'></div>于彼高冈。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1364187_comment'></div>盖天子之孝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364187_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1364187", 1364187, onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364187", 1364187, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>太阴</span>望兮圆魄皎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364187_comment'></div>阊阖开兮凉风袅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364187_comment'></div>四海澄兮百川皛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364187_comment'></div>阴阳肃兮天地窅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364187_comment'></div>扫离宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364187_comment'></div>清重閤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364187_comment'></div>设皇邸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364187_comment'></div>张翠幕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364187_comment'></div>鸾飞凤翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364187_comment'></div>睒晹<span onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1364187", 1364187, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>妙物</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364187_comment'></div>何造化之多端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364187_comment'></div>青莲吐而非夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364187_comment'></div>赪果摇而不寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364187_comment'></div>铜铁银锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364187_comment'></div>璆琳琅玕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364187_comment'></div>映以甘泉之玉树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364187_comment'></div>冠以承露之金盘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364187_comment'></div>宪章三极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364187_comment'></div>仪形万类。<div onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1364187", 1364187, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>安贞</span>兮象地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364187_comment'></div>殚怪力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364187_comment'></div>穷神异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364187_comment'></div>少君王子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364187_comment'></div>掣曳兮若来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364187_comment'></div>玉女瑶姬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364187_comment'></div>翩跹兮必至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364187_comment'></div>鸣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1364187", 1364187, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>鹔鹴</span>与鸑鷟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364187_comment'></div>舞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1364187", 1364187, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>鹍鸡</span>与翡翠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364187_comment'></div>毒龙拿兮赫然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364187_comment'></div>狂象奔兮沈醉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364187_comment'></div>怖魍魉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364187_comment'></div>潜魑魅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364187_comment'></div>离娄明目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364187_comment'></div>不足见其精微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364187_comment'></div>匠石洗心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364187_comment'></div>不足徵其奥秘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364187_comment'></div>缤缤纷纷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364187_comment'></div>氤氤氲氲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364187_comment'></div>五色成文若荣光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364187_comment'></div>休气发彩于重云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364187_comment'></div>茜茜粲粲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364187_comment'></div>焕焕烂烂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364187_comment'></div>三光壮观若合璧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364187_comment'></div>连珠<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_55_1364187", 1364187, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>耿耀</span>于长汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364187_comment'></div>夫其远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364187_comment'></div>天台杰起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364187_comment'></div>绕之以赤霞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364187_comment'></div>夫其近也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364187_comment'></div>削成孤峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364187_comment'></div>覆之以莲花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364187_comment'></div>晃兮瑶台之帝室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364187_comment'></div>赩兮<span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364187_comment'></div>上诸天于大梵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364187_comment'></div>其广也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364187_comment'></div>遍法界于恒沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364187_comment'></div>上可以荐元符于七庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364187_comment'></div>下可以纳群动于三车者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364187_comment'></div>于是乎腾声名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364187_comment'></div>列部伍。<div id='poem_sentence_73_1364187_comment'></div>左苍龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364187_comment'></div>右白虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364187_comment'></div>环卫匝。<div id='poem_sentence_128_1364187_comment'></div>大夫学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364187_comment'></div>再拜稽首而言曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364187_comment'></div>圣人之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364187_comment'></div>中于礼神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364187_comment'></div>终于法轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364187_comment'></div>武尽美矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364187_comment'></div>周命惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364187_comment'></div>圣神皇帝于是乎唯寂唯静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364187_comment'></div>无营无欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364187_comment'></div>寿命如天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364187_comment'></div>德音如玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364187_comment'></div>任贤相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364187_comment'></div>惇风俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364187_comment'></div>远佞人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364187_comment'></div>措刑狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364187_comment'></div>省游宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364187_comment'></div>披图箓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364187_comment'></div>捐珠玑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364187_comment'></div>宝菽粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364187_comment'></div>罢官之无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364187_comment'></div>恤人之不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364187_comment'></div>鼓天地之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_185_1364187", 1364187, "Clauses/185/Comments/0")'>化淳</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364187_comment'></div>作皇王之轨躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364187_comment'></div>太阳夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364187_comment'></div>乘舆归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364187_comment'></div>下端闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364187_comment'></div>入紫微。</div><div id='poem_sentence_190_1364187_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
三台（郪县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4bd71c7c126743888c47a1385ee529ee_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4bd71c7c126743888c47a1385ee529ee");'><span id='4bd71c7c126743888c47a1385ee529ee_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=685&endYear=685')">685年9;10月</a>　秋冬,出为梓州司法参军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=686&endYear=686')">686年1月</a>　正月,在梓州参军任,为郪县县令陆某作祭文。作品：《为梓州官属祭陆郪县文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷10第172页。）</span><div id='poem_1364264' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364264' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364264?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为梓州官属祭陆郪县文</a><span class='authorDate'>（686年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364264")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364264_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364264'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364264'>维垂拱二年太岁丙戌正月壬寅朔二十二日癸亥。长史刘某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364264_comment'></div>谨以清酌庶羞之奠。敬祭陆明府之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364264_comment'></div>夫万里之别。犹使饮泪成血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364264_comment'></div>思德音之断绝。况百年之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364264_comment'></div>能不忧心如薰。想公子兮氛氲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364264_comment'></div>惟彼积德。挺生夫君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364264_comment'></div>天垂白气。地发黄云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364264_comment'></div>江则有汜。为国之纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364264_comment'></div>君传其政。爱人如子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364264_comment'></div>山则有梁。镇兹一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364264_comment'></div>君宏其道。视人如伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364264_comment'></div>久劳于外。路阻且长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364264_comment'></div>曾未期月。人之云亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364264_comment'></div>呜乎哀哉。哀哀弱嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364264_comment'></div>朝暮一溢。皎皎孀妻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364264_comment'></div>颓乎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1364264", 1364264, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>下室</span>。蜀门如剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364264_comment'></div>长安如日。归路何从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364264_comment'></div>我心如疾。呜乎哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364264_comment'></div>凡我在位。羁官边城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364264_comment'></div>共戮力兮谁言死生。思其人兮造其户庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364264_comment'></div>恍无见兮寂无声。称觞兮酹酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364264_comment'></div>心折兮骨惊。呜乎哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364264_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1364264_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=686&endYear=686')">686年1月</a>　与梓州长史刘延嗣有唱和,作《和刘长史答十九兄》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷2第30页。）</span><div id='poem_33041' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_9_33041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_33041'>鼓鼙鸣九域，风火集重闉。<div id='poem_sentence_10_33041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_33041", 33041, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>精诚</span>动天地，忠义感明神。<div id='poem_sentence_16_33041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_33041'>怪鸟俄<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作来）</span>垂翼，修蛇竟暴鳞。<div id='poem_sentence_17_33041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_33041'>来朝拜<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作报）</span>休命，述职下梁<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作良）</span>岷。<div id='poem_sentence_18_33041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_33041'>善政驰金马，嘉声绕玉轮。<div id='poem_sentence_19_33041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_33041'>三荆忽有赠，四海更相亲。<div id='poem_sentence_20_33041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_33041'>宫徵谐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_33041", 33041, id='poem_sentence_21_33041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_33041'>山川遥满目，零露坐沾巾。<div id='poem_sentence_22_33041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_33041'>友爱光天下，恩波浃后尘。<div id='poem_sentence_23_33041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_33041'>懦夫仰高节，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(196, "poem_sentence_24_33041")'>下里</span>继阳春。<div id='poem_sentence_24_33041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_33041'></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_33041_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=686&endYear=686')">686年</a>　为昭武校尉曹通撰神道碑。作品：《唐昭武校尉曹君神道碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷8第132页。）</span><div id='poem_1364245' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364245' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364245?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐昭武校尉曹君神道碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（686年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364245")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364245_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364245'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364245'>君讳通。字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364245_comment'></div>其先沛国谯人也。近代因官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364245_comment'></div>遂居于瓜州之长乐县。故今为县人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364245_comment'></div>颛顼高阳之子孙。曹叔振铎之苗裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364245_comment'></div>山河白马。汉丞相开一代之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364245_comment'></div>谯沛黄龙。魏武帝定三分之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364245_comment'></div>承家恤允。岳峙星罗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364245_comment'></div>居雍州之西境。断匈奴之右臂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364245_comment'></div>门容驷马。旌旗玉塞之雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364245_comment'></div>坐列三貂。人物金行之秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364245_comment'></div>祖某。隐居不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364245_comment'></div>父显。荡寇将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364245_comment'></div>河庭宝玉。广都鸾凤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364245_comment'></div>或闾阎之内。礼敌于诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364245_comment'></div>或枹鼓之间。威振于千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364245_comment'></div>功则可大。以官族而为官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364245_comment'></div>德亦不孤。惟将门而有将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364245_comment'></div>君天才卓越。雄略纵横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364245_comment'></div>陶谦性好于幡旗。王浚志在于长戟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364245_comment'></div>东方谏议口诵孙吴。诸葛武侯坐吟梁甫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364245_comment'></div>属有隋之末。四海分崩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364245_comment'></div>皇运之初。三光草昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364245_comment'></div>五星同聚。田横犹在于海中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364245_comment'></div>九代飞荣。隗嚣尚屯于陇右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364245_comment'></div>贺拔盛操符誓众。斩木称兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364245_comment'></div>以被发左衽之馀。负梼杌穷奇之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364245_comment'></div>遂欲驱驰我塞北。挠乱我河西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364245_comment'></div>天子不怿于庙堂。鼓其雷电。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364245_comment'></div>使者相望于道路。申其吊伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364245_comment'></div>武德元年。乃诏侍中杨仁恭出使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364245_comment'></div>先之以德义。陈之以兵甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364245_comment'></div>七旬干羽。不藉有苗之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364245_comment'></div>万国侯王。坐见防风之戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364245_comment'></div>君深知逆顺。独断胸怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364245_comment'></div>去危即安。转祸为福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364245_comment'></div>非如马援遨游二帝之都。不学窦融自保三分之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364245_comment'></div>敕授昭武校尉。鲜卑丑类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364245_comment'></div>慕容残孽。迁于大棘之城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364245_comment'></div>止于小兰之介。虽谓其群下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364245_comment'></div>愿闻礼于上京。而拜于将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364245_comment'></div>遂誇大于诸国。贞观八年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364245_comment'></div>诏特进代国公李靖为行军大总管。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1364245", 1364245, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>登坛拜将</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364245_comment'></div>授钺行师。开太一之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1364245", 1364245, "Clauses/85/Comments/0")'>三门</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364245_comment'></div>闭阴符之六甲。决胜于俎豆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364245_comment'></div>然后折冲万里。信贤如腹心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364245_comment'></div>故能匡正八极。君当仁不让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364245_comment'></div>闻义则行。从王粲之戎旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364245_comment'></div>弃班超之笔研。系单于之颈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364245_comment'></div>有类长沙。斩楼兰之王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364245_comment'></div>更加平乐。诏除上骑都尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364245_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_50_1364245", 1364245, "Clauses/100/Comments/0")'>车师</span>旧国。俯枕前庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364245_comment'></div>戊己遗墟。斜连后壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364245_comment'></div>负天山而板荡。拥蒲海而虔刘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364245_comment'></div>圣人之德。非欲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1364245", 1364245, "Clauses/107/Comments/0")'>穷兵黩武</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364245_comment'></div>王者之师。盖为夷凶靖乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364245_comment'></div>十四年。诏兵部尚书侯君集为行军大总管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364245_comment'></div>军营玉帐。武略珠韬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364245_comment'></div>旌旗蔽于日月。金鼓闻于天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364245_comment'></div>安人保大。实凭帷幄之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364245_comment'></div>斩将搴旗。咸藉武夫之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364245_comment'></div>君缅怀高义。思报国恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364245_comment'></div>从来六郡之子。是为万人之敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364245_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_1364245", 1364245, "Clauses/124/Comments/0")'>梯冲</span>所及。披靡坚城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364245_comment'></div>矛戟所临。野无横阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364245_comment'></div>一举而清海外。再战而涤<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_64_1364245", 1364245, "Clauses/129/Comments/0")'>河源</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364245_comment'></div>饮至策勋。抑惟恒授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364245_comment'></div>诏除上柱国。君备尝艰阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364245_comment'></div>频有战功。天子闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364245_comment'></div>累加徵辟。慕田畴之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364245_comment'></div>羞卖卢龙之塞。高鲁连之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364245_comment'></div>请从沧海之游。遂乃散发乡亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364245_comment'></div>拂衣丘壑。为赵魏之老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364245_comment'></div>在羲皇之年。关内诸公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364245_comment'></div>深知郭解。洛阳人物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364245_comment'></div>高谈剧孟。家僮有礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364245_comment'></div>皆使拜宾。门客多才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364245_comment'></div>咸能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_76_1364245", 1364245, "Clauses/152/Comments/0")'>市义</span>。南宫养老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364245_comment'></div>坐闻鸠杖之荣。东岳游魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364245_comment'></div>俄见<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_78_1364245", 1364245, "Clauses/156/Comments/0")'>鹤书</span>之召。以龙朔元年某月某日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364245_comment'></div>终于里第。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364245_comment'></div>夫人某官之女也。沅湘降祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364245_comment'></div>河洛腾休。符玉石之坚贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364245_comment'></div>贯风霜之惨烈。镜飞天上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364245_comment'></div>窥祥凤于银台。剑动星文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364245_comment'></div>秘蛟龙于玉匣。以某年某月日终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364245_comment'></div>越某年月日。合葬于某原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364245_comment'></div>君孝实因心。忠为令德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364245_comment'></div>鲜花匝树。尽兄弟之欢娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364245_comment'></div>好鸟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_88_1364245", 1364245, "Clauses/176/Comments/0")'>鸣林</span>。展交游之宴喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364245_comment'></div>太初朗月。俯照金鞍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364245_comment'></div>叔夜清风。来生宝剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364245_comment'></div>故能战必胜。攻必取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364245_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_1364245", 1364245, "Clauses/184/Comments/0")'>西零</span>种族。遥惮武臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364245_comment'></div>北漠酋豪。见称飞将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364245_comment'></div>虽死之日。犹生之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364245_comment'></div>园令独慕于相如。汉帝长怀于李牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364245_comment'></div>长子游击将军和政府右果毅都尉上柱国永雄次子朝散郎行西州柳中县主簿上骑都尉知君等。三馀广学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364245_comment'></div>百战雄才。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_97_1364245", 1364245, "Clauses/195/Comments/0")'>就养</span>之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364245_comment'></div>兼申爱敬。慎终之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364245_comment'></div>不忘哀戚。虽雨崩防墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364245_comment'></div>无孔子之格言。而水齧前和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364245_comment'></div>有文王之故事。即以某年月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364245_comment'></div>改葬于木城之平原。长妇某氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364245_comment'></div>即永雄之妻也。某官之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364245_comment'></div>柔风淑誉。习礼闻诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364245_comment'></div>上奉舅姑。旁睦娣姒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364245_comment'></div>温家之妇。方欢白玉之台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364245_comment'></div>卢氏之妻。空对黄金之碗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364245_comment'></div>先以永淳元年某月日终。至是即陪窆于茔内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364245_comment'></div>右翊卫宏轨。兵图日用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364245_comment'></div>剑术天知。六郡许其良家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364245_comment'></div>三川养其声利。思宏祖德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364245_comment'></div>愿叙家风。托无愧之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364245_comment'></div>跋涉载劳于千仞。访他山之石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364245_comment'></div>东西向踰于万里。炯效官昌运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364245_comment'></div>负谴明时。始以东宫学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364245_comment'></div>出为梓州司法。倾盖相逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364245_comment'></div>当仁不让。庶使见曹娥之碣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364245_comment'></div>杨修叹其好词。读元寿之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364245_comment'></div>高祖称其佳作。其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364245_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_120_1364245'>大矣丞相。天地寅亮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364245_comment'></div>烝哉王侯。子孙蕃昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364245_comment'></div>条分叶散。源浚流长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364245_comment'></div>金城北峙。玉关西侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364245_comment'></div>山泽骈罗。衣冠辐凑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364245_comment'></div>降神生德。兴贤诞秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364245_comment'></div>曰万人英。材标国桢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364245_comment'></div>髫年学剑。丱岁论兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364245_comment'></div>以身许国。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_128_1364245", 1364245, "Clauses/257/Comments/0")'>东讨西征</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364245_comment'></div>皇家启圣。拨乱反正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364245_comment'></div>逆贼游魂。不恭王命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364245_comment'></div>亦既授首。河西大定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364245_comment'></div>蕞尔湟中。车书未同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364245_comment'></div>帝赫斯怒。攒其英雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364245_comment'></div>风行电转。谷静山空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364245_comment'></div>二庭遗孽。交河路绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364245_comment'></div>天子闻鼙。元戎按节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364245_comment'></div>王师无战。海外有截。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364245_comment'></div>归我田庐。功成不居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364245_comment'></div>岁云秋矣。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_139_1364245", 1364245, "Clauses/279/Comments/0")'>日月其除</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364245_comment'></div>寿非金石。命也何如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364245_comment'></div>孝乎兄弟。葬之以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364245_comment'></div>蓼蓼者莪。人生苦多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364245_comment'></div>言犹在耳。邈若山河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364245_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_144_1364245_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=687&endYear=687')">687年</a>　在梓州司法参军任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=688&endYear=688')">688年4月</a>　四月,应郪县县令窦兢作《梓州惠义寺重阁铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷5第72页。）</span><div id='poem_1364234' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364234' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364234?labeling=true' target='_blank'>梓州惠<span class='inlineComment2'>（集作慧）</span>义寺重阁铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364234")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364234_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1364234'>大辰之岁。正阳之月。有郪县宰扶风窦竞。字思慎。昭宣令德。光阐化猷。庶政惟和。万民以理。闲庭不扰。退食自公。远览形势。虔心净域。乃与禅师释智海忘言契道。寓目于长平之山。援飞茎。陟峭崿。削成千仞。壁立万寻。俯观大地。仅如枣叶。下望须弥。裁同芥子。飞流滴沥而成响。乔树璀璨而垂荣。玉堂石室。千门相似。璧殿珠毫。十方皆现。慷慨榱桷之未立。吁嗟栋宇之莫修。不舍有为。取诸大壮。观夫左龙角。右参旗。前太微。后营室。骈罗列以杂沓。瑟萧条而清泠。上磊落以晃朗。下泓澄而叆叇。参参差差。森森纚纚。千栌万栱。乍合乍离。茜茜粲粲。绚绚焕焕。六采五章。或同或散。莽如天覆。矗似云平。金火合舍于垂珠。日月相望于衔璧。璇墀扣砌。平接太阶。玉户金扉。俯临阊阖。曳红日。舒丹霞。丰隆为雷。砰铿訇于轩槛。列缺为电。翕曶霍于庭除。寒暑隔阂于墙垣。虹霓回带于廊庑。仰之不极。目炫炫而丧精。登之无阶。心皇皇而失度。若士翔九垓之表。仍不逮于上荣。大章穷四海之间。犹未离于前墄。借如梵天之宅。释帝之宫。两曜城池。五云楼观。轮王所处。纯金为说法之堂。诸佛所游。众香作经行之地。亦未可同年而语也。夫黄金镂榜。曾不若四摄之门。青石为墙。曾不若三空之舍。殚百工之力。建七宝之楼。岂徒然哉。良有以也。故如来神力。且观严净。道师方便。化作一城。事有古而可以质于今。言有大而可以徵于小。是则毗耶四会。俱发道心。险路众人。咸知宝所。其铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1364234_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364234'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364234'>长平山兮建重阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364234_comment'></div>上穹窿兮下磅礡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364234_comment'></div>纷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1364234", 1364234, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>被丽</span>兮骈交错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364234_comment'></div>严色相兮冲寂寞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364234_comment'></div>谁所为兮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1364234", 1364234, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>天匠</span>作。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1364234_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=688&endYear=688')">688年</a>　秋,秩满,将归洛,作《梓州官僚赞》,其中包括杨炯自己,共二十八人。<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷10第176页。）</span><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
奉节
-----detail

id='poem_sentence_1_33053'>山路绕羊肠，江城镇鱼腹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_33053_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_33053'><span class='link' id='poem_sentence_10_33053_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_33056' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_33056' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/33056?labeling=true' target='_blank'>巫峡</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年9;10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_33056")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_33056_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_33056'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_33056'>三峡七百里，唯言<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_33056", 33056, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>巫峡</span>长。<div id='poem_sentence_0_33056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_33056'>重岩窅不极，叠嶂凌苍苍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_33056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_33056'>绝壁横天险，莓苔烂锦章。<div id='poem_sentence_2_33056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_33056'>入夜分明见，无风波浪狂。<div id='poem_sentence_3_33056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_33056'>忠信吾所蹈，泛舟亦何伤。<div id='poem_sentence_4_33056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_33056'>可以涉砥柱，可以浮吕梁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_33056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_33056'>美人今何在，灵芝徒有<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作自）</span>芳。<div id='poem_sentence_6_33056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_33056'>山空夜猿啸，征客泪沾裳。<div id='poem_sentence_7_33056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_33056'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_33056_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
宜昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c95e5b04b33246d9a0abfd5f45309633_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c95e5b04b33246d9a0abfd5f45309633");'><span id='c95e5b04b33246d9a0abfd5f45309633_link' class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_33055")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_33055_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_33055'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' id='poem_sentence_0_33055'>绝壁耸万仞，长波射千里。<div id='poem_sentence_0_33055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_33055'>盘薄荆之门，滔滔<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(6480, "poem_sentence_1_33055")'>南国纪</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_33055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_33055'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_33055", 33055, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>楚都</span>昔全盛，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_33055", 33055, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>高丘</span>烜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_33055", 33055, "Clauses/5/Comments/1")'>望祀</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_33055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_33055'>秦兵一旦侵，夷陵火潜起。<div id='poem_sentence_3_33055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='inlineComment2'>（一作然）</span>，孟门终已矣。<div id='poem_sentence_5_33055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_33055'>自古天地辟，流为峡中水。<div id='poem_sentence_6_33055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_33055'>行旅相赠言，风涛无极已。<div id='poem_sentence_7_33055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_33055'>及余践斯地，瑰奇信为美。<div id='poem_sentence_8_33055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_33055'>江山若有灵，千载伸知己。<div -----title
衢州（盈川）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d32f3d26ad714012ba31c5185cd9e41b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d32f3d26ad714012ba31c5185cd9e41b");'><span id='d32f3d26ad714012ba31c5185cd9e41b_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=692&endYear=692')">692年9;10月</a>　秋冬,出为盈川令,张说作诗赠行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=693&endYear=693')">693年</a>　在盈川县令任.春,作《大周明威将军梁公神道碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷6第86页。《杨炯集》作《后周明威将军梁公神道碑》）</span><div id='poem_1364249' class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364249")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364249_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364249'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364249'>盖闻君为元首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364249_comment'></div>臣作股肱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364249_comment'></div>或论道三槐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364249_comment'></div>或折冲千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364249_comment'></div>至有道存俎豆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364249_comment'></div>艺总干戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364249_comment'></div>高视翰墨之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364249_comment'></div>独布爪牙之旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364249_comment'></div>究青编于学府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364249_comment'></div>业有多闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364249_comment'></div>受黄石之兵符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364249_comment'></div>算无遗策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364249_comment'></div>故得九功咸叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364249_comment'></div>七德攸彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364249_comment'></div>文武不坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364249_comment'></div>公实兼美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364249_comment'></div>公讳待宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364249_comment'></div>安定临泾人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364249_comment'></div>竦以英才远迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364249_comment'></div>知州县之徒劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364249_comment'></div>鸿以抗节遐征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364249_comment'></div>览帝京而有作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364249_comment'></div>由是五噫标兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364249_comment'></div>播金石而腾徽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364249_comment'></div>七贵承荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364249_comment'></div>绾银黄而謺茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364249_comment'></div>贞规盛烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364249_comment'></div>映史凝图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364249_comment'></div>粗纪咏歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364249_comment'></div>无俟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1364249", 1364249, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>详确</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364249_comment'></div>高祖御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364249_comment'></div>后魏驸马都尉侍中少保金紫光禄大夫扬州总管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364249_comment'></div>赠太尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364249_comment'></div>谥昭公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364249_comment'></div>食邑三千户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364249_comment'></div>银榜增辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364249_comment'></div>玉壶流渥。<div id='poem_sentence_38_1364249_comment'></div>既而幽垄埋魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364249_comment'></div>终降<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1364249", 1364249, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>槐庭</span>之赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364249_comment'></div>高门纳驷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364249_comment'></div>式居茅社之封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364249_comment'></div>曾祖睿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364249_comment'></div>宇文周驸马都尉鄜秦二州总管光禄大夫兵部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364249_comment'></div>隋益州总管蒋国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364249_comment'></div>赠司空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364249_comment'></div>食邑三千户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364249_comment'></div>白水时清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364249_comment'></div>乳虎之谣行息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364249_comment'></div>禄符垂翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364249_comment'></div>叩马之谏必申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364249_comment'></div>加以主西序之群英。<div id='poem_sentence_70_1364249_comment'></div>隋左千牛备身骊山府上骑柱国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364249_comment'></div>皇朝丰王府咨议云州司马冀州长史蒋国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364249_comment'></div>侣明月而飞文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364249_comment'></div>北土行康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364249_comment'></div>望浮云而展足。<div id='poem_sentence_104_1364249_comment'></div>誉满寰中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364249_comment'></div>声盖天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364249_comment'></div>而学优将仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364249_comment'></div>允属名家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364249_comment'></div>欲升鸿渐之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364249_comment'></div>终伫鹤鸣之闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364249_comment'></div>以皇朝麟德二年补左亲卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364249_comment'></div>从资例也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364249_comment'></div>属金甲出战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364249_comment'></div>玉帐论兵。<div id='poem_sentence_125_1364249_comment'></div>我有力焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364249_comment'></div>俯洽恩波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364249_comment'></div>泛承勋级。<div id='poem_sentence_130_1364249_comment'></div>命舛数奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364249_comment'></div>虽沾勒石之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364249_comment'></div>未展披坚之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364249_comment'></div>嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364249_comment'></div>扬子云之才藻。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_343_1364249_comment'></div>入司宫掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_344_1364249_comment'></div><span class='link' id='poem_sentence_346_1364249_comment'></div>式重其骏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_347_1364249_comment'></div>载怀斯癖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_348_1364249_comment'></div>我马既良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_349_1364249_comment'></div>我军既雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_350_1364249_comment'></div>折冲千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_351_1364249_comment'></div>趋奉九重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_352_1364249_comment'></div>行承芝诰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_353_1364249_comment'></div>坐启茅封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_354_1364249_comment'></div>恨深负米。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_355_1364249_comment'></div>荣暨击钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_356_1364249_comment'></div>爰持<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_357_1364249", 1364249, "Clauses/357/Comments/0")'>戒律</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_357_1364249_comment'></div>思答慈容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_358_1364249_comment'></div>将福有徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_359_1364249_comment'></div>谓仁必寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_360_1364249_comment'></div>如何淑德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_361_1364249_comment'></div>遭此凶咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_362_1364249_comment'></div>孺慕崩心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_363_1364249_comment'></div>茕嫠缩首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_364_1364249_comment'></div>夜泉扃闭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_365_1364249_comment'></div>天长地久。</div><div id='poem_sentence_366_1364249_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='7c72af87ea58477f9632268a367a7115_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7c72af87ea58477f9632268a367a7115");'><span id='7c72af87ea58477f9632268a367a7115_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=693&endYear=693')">693年</a>，44岁</div><div id='7c72af87ea58477f9632268a367a7115' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=693&endYear=693')">693年</a>　卒于官.殁而无子,由其弟运灵柩归葬华阴.经洛阳时,友人郭氏、崔氏（崔融）曾来祭奠.文集由宋之问整理,宋氏并助卜葬诸事。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
丽水（括苍）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='681c59281c7645a3ae1cb26e9e02d402_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("681c59281c7645a3ae1cb26e9e02d402");'><span id='681c59281c7645a3ae1cb26e9e02d402_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=693&endYear=693')">693年</a>，44岁</div><div id='681c59281c7645a3ae1cb26e9e02d402' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=693&endYear=693')">693年</a>　在盈川县令任,曾至括州,作有《李舍人山亭诗序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐明霞点校《卢照邻集杨炯集》中华书局1980年版卷3第43页。）</span><div id='poem_1364196' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364196' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364196?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李舍人山亭诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（693年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17397, "初唐", "杨炯", "poem_title_1364196")'>杨炯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364196_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364196'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364196'>永嘉有高阳公山亭者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364196_comment'></div>今为李舍人别墅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364196_comment'></div>廊宇重复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364196_comment'></div>楼台左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364196_comment'></div>烟霞栖梁栋之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364196_comment'></div>竹树在汀洲之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364196_comment'></div>龟山对出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364196_comment'></div>背东武而飞来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364196_comment'></div>鹤阜相临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364196_comment'></div>向东吴而不进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364196_comment'></div>青溪数曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364196_comment'></div>赤岩千丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364196_comment'></div>寥廓兮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1364196", 1364196, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>惚恍</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364196_comment'></div>似蓬岭之难行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364196_comment'></div>深邃兮眇然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364196_comment'></div>若桃源之失路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364196_comment'></div>信可谓赤县幽栖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364196_comment'></div>黄图胜景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364196_comment'></div>从来八子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364196_comment'></div>辟高阳之邑居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364196_comment'></div>今日四郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364196_comment'></div>逢舍人之置驿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364196_comment'></div>故知樊家失业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364196_comment'></div>遂作庾公之园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364196_comment'></div>习氏不游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364196_comment'></div>终成濮阴之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364196_comment'></div>其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364196_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1364196", 1364196, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>凝脂点漆</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364196_comment'></div>琼树瑶林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364196_comment'></div>学富文史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364196_comment'></div>言成<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1364196", 1364196, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>准的</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364196_comment'></div>葭莩为汉帝之亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364196_comment'></div>凡蒋是周公之裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364196_comment'></div>田孟尝之待客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364196_comment'></div>照饭无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364196_comment'></div>孔文举之邀欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364196_comment'></div>樽中自溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364196_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1364196", 1364196, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>三冬</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1364196", 1364196, "Clauses/37/Comments/1")'>事隙</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364196_comment'></div>五日归休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364196_comment'></div>奏金石而满堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364196_comment'></div>召琳琅而触目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364196_comment'></div>心焉而醉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364196_comment'></div>德焉而饱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364196_comment'></div>大隐朝韨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364196_comment'></div>本无车马之喧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364196_comment'></div>不出户庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364196_comment'></div>坐得云霄之致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364196_comment'></div>于是乎百年无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364196_comment'></div>万事徒劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364196_comment'></div>唯谈笑可以遣平生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364196_comment'></div>唯文词可以陈<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_50_1364196", 1364196, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>心赏</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364196_comment'></div>既因良会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364196_comment'></div>咸请赋诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364196_comment'></div>虽向之所欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364196_comment'></div>已为陈迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364196_comment'></div>俾千载之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364196_comment'></div>感于斯文。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1364196_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
